### [1] [Auto-Conditioned Frank-Wolfe Algorithms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15512)
*Khanh-Hung Giang-Tran,Soroosh Shafiee,Nam Ho-Nguyen*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种全自动条件化的Frank-Wolfe型方法框架，用局部Lipschitz估计替代全局光滑常数，无需先验知识即可实现闭环比长选择，在非凸和凸设定下均保持收敛保证，并在线搜索方法上取得显著实践改进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典Frank-Wolfe方法的闭环比长规则需要全局光滑常数先验知识，而线搜索变体虽避免此要求但增加了函数评估次数和实现开销。本文旨在消除对全局光滑常数的依赖，同时保留闭环比长规则的简洁性和高效性。

Method: 提出自动条件化框架，利用沿迭代轨迹的一阶信息估计局部Lipschitz常数，替代全局Lipschitz常数用于闭环比长；该框架统一了标准Frank-Wolfe、Matching Pursuit、pairwise Frank-Wolfe和away-step Frank-Wolfe等多种投影-free子程序。

Result: 在非凸设定下建立了收敛到驻点的保证；在凸设定下恢复了标准次线性收敛率；结合额外结构假设时，可加速收敛速率；数值实验表明相比线搜索方法有显著实践改进。

Conclusion: 所提框架在不需要全局光滑常数先验知识的前提下，成功实现了闭环比长规则的适应性和简洁性，兼顾了理论收敛保证与实际性能优势。

Abstract: Frank-Wolfe methods are projection-free algorithms for constrained optimization whose practical performance often depends critically on the choice of step size. Classical closed-loop step-size rules typically require prior knowledge of a global smoothness constant, while line-search variants avoid this requirement at the cost of additional function evaluations and implementation overhead. In this paper, we develop a fully auto-conditioned framework for Frank-Wolfe-type methods. The framework replaces the global Lipschitz constant in closed-loop step sizes with a local Lipschitz estimator computed from first-order information along the iterates. We show that this abstraction captures several important projection-free subroutines, including standard Frank-Wolfe, Matching Pursuit, pairwise Frank-Wolfe, and away-step Frank-Wolfe. For the resulting general class of methods, we establish convergence to stationary points in the nonconvex setting and recover the standard sublinear convergence guarantees in the convex setting, without requiring prior knowledge of a global smoothness constant. We further show that, when specialized to particular Frank-Wolfe variants and combined with additional structural assumptions, the same auto-conditioned framework yields accelerated convergence rates. Numerical experiments demonstrate that the proposed methods provide substantial practical improvements over line-search-based alternatives, highlighting the benefits of adapting to local curvature while retaining the simplicity of closed-loop step-size rules.

</details>


### [2] [Stochastic Non-Smooth Convex Optimization with Unbounded Gradients](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15522)
*Dmitry Kovalev*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文针对非光滑优化中梯度一致有界的限制性假设，提出了更符合实际的广义Lipschitz函数类（梯度范数由最优性间隙的仿射函数界定）。通过分析多种现有算法，发现带裁剪更新的AdamW在凸随机广义Lipschitz优化问题上全局收敛速度最优，超越了SGD和AdaGrad。研究还揭示了AdamW指数加权梯度累积的关键作用，并将结果扩展到广义光滑性假设、对角/矩阵预条件及quasar-凸设置。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有非光滑优化理论基于梯度一致有界的限制性假设，与实际问题不符。本文旨在提出更现实的广义Lipschitz函数类，并回答何种算法能在该类问题上取得最优全局收敛率。

Method: 对多种现有算法（SGD、AdaGrad、AdamW等）进行新的收敛性分析，重点研究带裁剪更新的AdamW，分析其指数加权梯度累积机制，并扩展到广义光滑性、预条件及quasar-凸等场景。

Result: 带裁剪更新的AdamW在理论上优于SGD和AdaGrad；指数加权梯度累积（而非简单平均）起关键作用；该方法在广义光滑性假设下具有通用性且收敛率更优；分析扩展到对角/矩阵预条件和quasar-凸设置。

Conclusion: AdamW（带裁剪更新）是求解广义Lipschitz优化问题的最优随机优化算法之一，其指数加权机制至关重要，且方法具有良好的可扩展性。

Abstract: Much of the existing theory on first-order non-smooth optimization is built on a restrictive assumption that the gradients of the objective function are uniformly bounded. We introduce a much more realistic class of generalized Lipschitz functions, where the gradient norms are bounded by an affine function of the optimality gap. We then ask a natural question: what algorithm achieves the best global convergence rates for solving convex stochastic generalized Lipschitz optimization problems? To address this, we develop a new convergence analysis for several existing algorithms and find that AdamW with clipped updates, theoretically outperforms other popular stochastic optimization methods, such as SGD and AdaGrad. Moreover, our analysis establishes the critical role of AdamW's exponentially weighted gradient accumulation, as opposed to simple averaging. We further show that clipped AdamW is universal and achieves improved rates under the popular generalized smoothness assumption, analyze the convergence of clipped AdamW with diagonal and matrix preconditioners, and extend our results to the quasar-convex setting.

</details>


### [3] [Distributionally Robust Nash Equilibrium Seeking with Partial Observations and Distributed Communication](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15534)
*Nirabhra Mandal,Sonia Martínez*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文研究随机单次博弈中，智能体在无法获知随机变量真实分布、仅有有限i.i.d.样本的情况下，通过分布鲁棒博弈框架（Wasserstein球）寻求分布鲁棒纳什均衡（DRoNE），并提出一种分布式惯性支撑更优响应超梯度算法（d-ISBRAG）在有向通信网络中求解该均衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实博弈中，智能体的效用依赖于随机环境，但决策者通常无法获知随机变量的真实分布，仅能获得有限样本。经典随机博弈假设已知分布，而实际中分布不确定性可能导致均衡偏离。作者希望通过分布鲁棒优化（在Wasserstein球内最大化最坏情况期望效用）来刻画这种不确定性，并研究相应均衡的存在性、逼近性质及分布式求解方法。

Method: 首先建立分布鲁棒博弈模型，在Wasserstein球内定义智能体的最坏情况期望效用；给出分布鲁棒纳什均衡（DRoNE）存在的条件；分析DRoNE与随机博弈纳什均衡（NE）的逼近关系。提出ISBRAG算法（惯性支撑更优响应上升超梯度动力学）求解DRoNE，要求博弈具有"友善超梯度"性质。在此基础上设计分布式版本d-ISBRAG，通过动态一致性估计子在有向通信网络中估计他人策略，并分别处理个体样本和共享样本两种情形。

Result: 给出了分布鲁棒博弈存在非空DRoNE的条件；刻画了DRoNE与NE之间的逼近误差界；提出了ISBRAG及其分布式版本d-ISBRAG算法，可在有向通信网络下收敛到DRoNE；在共享样本情形下，通过对分布鲁棒优化问题进行可处理的重构，实现了分布式超梯度计算；仿真实验验证了算法有效性。

Conclusion: 本文为不确定环境下（有限样本、未知分布）的随机博弈提供了一套完整的理论分析与分布式求解框架，将分布鲁棒优化与博弈论有机结合，为多智能体系统在信息受限场景下的均衡决策提供了可行方案。

Abstract: In this work, we study stochastic one-shot games where agents' utilities depend on the collective strategy profiles of other agents as well as on some well-behaved randomness. While each decision-maker is agnostic to the random variable's underlying distribution, they have access to finitely many i.i.d. samples generated from it. We consider two cases: one where samples are shared; and another, more special one, where samples are individually accessible. To hedge against the unknown uncertainty, each agent plays a distributionally robust game and aims to maximize the worst-case expected utility over a Wasserstein ball around the sample average distribution. In this setting, we provide conditions under which the game has a non-empty set of distributionally robust Nash equilibria (DRoNE) and then characterize the closeness of the DRoNE set to the Nash equilibria (NE) of the associated stochastic game. We then propose an inertial, supported, better response, ascending supergradient dynamics ISBRAG that seeks the DRoNE's when the distributionally robust game possesses what we term as amicable supergradients. This forms the basis of a distributed version (d-ISBRAG) where agents estimate others' strategies by means of a dynamic consensus subroutine over a directed communication network. While initially the distributed algorithm works in the case where agents have individual samples, we later extend this to the case of shared observations under certain simplifying assumptions. This involves analyzing a tractable reformulation of the distributionally robust optimization problem and solving it in a distributed manner to compute the required supergradients. Simulations illustrate our results.

</details>


### [4] [Stochastic Mirror Descent under Iterate-Dependent Markov Noise: Analysis in the Asymptotic and Finite Time Regimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15538)
*Anik Kumar Paul,Shalabh Bhatnagar*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文研究决策变量影响采样分布且样本由状态依赖马尔可夫链生成的随机优化问题，分析了随机镜像下降算法在该设定下的收敛性，建立了凸与非凸问题下的几乎必然收敛和有限时间浓度界，样本复杂度在凸情形下匹配i.i.d.噪声下的经典速率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实际优化问题中，采样分布常依赖于决策变量，且样本通过状态依赖马尔可夫链生成，传统基于i.i.d.噪声的方法不再适用，需要建立新的理论框架。

Method: 分析随机镜像下降算法在迭代依赖马尔可夫噪声下的收敛性，利用Lipschitz连续性假设（无需可微性）证明几乎必然收敛，并对光滑目标导出有限时间浓度界。

Result: 凸情形下样本复杂度匹配i.i.d.噪声下的经典SMD速率；非凸情形下获得关于概率单纯形上黎曼梯度范数的样本复杂度界。

Conclusion: 建立了状态依赖马尔可夫噪声下随机镜像下降的统一收敛框架，揭示了其在凸和非凸区域中的行为。

Abstract: We study a stochastic optimization problem in which the sampling distribution depends on the decision variable, and the available samples are generated through an iterate-dependent Markov chain. Such settings arise naturally in problems with decision-dependent uncertainty; however, they introduce bias and temporal dependence, which render standard techniques developed for i.i.d.\ noise inapplicable. In this work, we analyze the stochastic mirror descent algorithm under iterate-dependent Markov noise. We first establish almost sure convergence for both convex and non-convex problems under the mild assumption of Lipschitz continuity of the objective function, without requiring differentiability. We then derive finite-time concentration bounds for smooth objectives. In the convex setting, the resulting sample complexity matches the classical rate of stochastic mirror descent under i.i.d.\ noise. In the non-convex setting, we obtain a sample complexity bound in terms of the norm of the Riemannian gradient over the probability simplex. Overall, our results establish a unified convergence framework for stochastic mirror descent with state-dependent Markov noise, and highlight its behavior in both convex and non-convex regimes.

</details>


### [5] [Spectral conjugate gradient projection methods for large-scale monotone equations without Lipschitz continuity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15570)
*Kabenge Hamiss,Mohammed Alshahrani,Mujahid N. Syed*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文提出两种用于大规模非线性单调方程组（带凸约束）的无导数投影方法，分别基于特征值优化的尺度矩阵改进最优Perry方法，以及基于谱Dai-Liao参数改进Hager-Zhang型共轭梯度投影方法。两种方法均保证充分下降条件，第一种方法在仅单调性条件下全局收敛，第二种方法在标准单调性和Lipschitz连续性假设下全局收敛。数值实验表明算法有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决大规模带凸约束的非线性单调方程组求解问题，现有无导数投影方法在收敛条件和实际效率上仍有改进空间，特别是无需Lipschitz连续性的全局收敛性保证。

Method: 将自适应谱参数融入经典共轭梯度框架：方法一通过特征值优化的缩放矩阵推广改进最优Perry方法；方法二通过谱Dai-Liao参数推广Hager-Zhang型共轭梯度投影方法。搜索方向独立于线搜索满足充分下降条件。

Result: 方法一在仅单调性假设下全局收敛（无需Lipschitz连续性）；方法二在单调性和Lipschitz连续性下全局收敛。在18个测试问题（维度高达120,000）及ℓ1正则化信号恢复和正则化逻辑回归应用中验证了有效性。

Conclusion: 提出的两种无导数投影方法在理论上具有更宽松的收敛条件，实践中对大规模凸约束非线性单调方程组有效，可应用于信号处理和机器学习中的正则化问题。

Abstract: We introduce two derivative-free projection methods for large-scale systems of nonlinear monotone equations subject to convex constraints. Both methods incorporate an adaptive spectral parameter into established conjugate gradient frameworks: the first generalizes the modified optimal Perry method via an eigenvalue-optimized scaling matrix, and the second generalizes the Hager--Zhang-type conjugate gradient projection method via a spectral Dai--Liao parameter. The resulting search directions satisfy a sufficient descent condition independent of the line search. For the first method, we establish global convergence under monotonicity alone, without requiring Lipschitz continuity of the mapping. For the second, global convergence holds under the standard monotonicity and Lipschitz continuity assumptions. Numerical experiments on 18 test problems across dimensions up to 120{,}000, together with applications to $\ell_1$-regularized signal recovery and regularized logistic regression, confirm the practical effectiveness of the proposed approach.

</details>


### [6] [Decomposition and Successive Decomposition Methods and Algorithms for Nonconvex Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15594)
*Yiqing Zhai,Ying Cui,Danny H. K. Tsang*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文针对现有非凸问题分解方法研究的不足，提出了适用于更一般分解结构的原始和对偶分解方法及逐次分解方法，这些方法能够利用分解结构、支持并行分布式实现、收敛到原问题的驻点，并在收敛性能与计算时间之间实现优越权衡，同时推广了凸问题的基本分解方法并扩展了非凸问题的现有分解方法，丰富了分解理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有非凸问题的分解方法研究不足，特别是缺乏处理带有耦合非线性等式约束的并行分解算法，且现有方法未能充分利用问题中的分解结构（即耦合变量和约束）。

Method: 提出了原始分解、对偶分解、逐次原始分解和逐次对偶分解方法及算法，利用分解结构，支持并行和分布式实现，推广到间接分解和两级分解方法。

Result: 所提方法能够找到原非凸问题的驻点，在收敛性能与计算时间之间实现优越权衡，并通过实例和数值结果验证了各自的价值。

Conclusion: 提出的分解和逐次分解方法推广了凸问题的基本分解方法，拓展了非凸问题的现有分解方法，共同丰富了分解理论。

Abstract: Existing results on decomposition methods and algorithms for nonconvex problems are minimal. Parallel decomposition algorithms do not exist for nonconvex problems with coupling nonlinear equality constraints. Besides, decomposition structures (i.e., coupling variables and constraints) are not fully exploited in designing decomposition methods and algorithms. In this paper, we consider nonconvex problems with decomposition structures that are more general than those handled in the existing literature. We propose primal and dual decomposition and successive primal and successive dual decomposition methods and algorithms for these nonconvex problems, which exploit decomposition structures, allow for parallel and distributed implementations, produce the original nonconvex problems' stationary points, and offer good opportunities to achieve superior tradeoff between convergence performance and computation time. Finally, we compare the proposed methods and algorithms, extend them to indirect and two-level decomposition methods and algorithms, and provide examples and numerical results to demonstrate their respective values. Notably, the proposed decomposition and successive decomposition methods and algorithms generalize the basic ones for convex problems, and the proposed successive decomposition methods and algorithms extend the existing ones for nonconvex problems, together enriching the decomposition theory.

</details>


### [7] [Travel-time tomography from mean field game dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15602)
*Longqiang Xu,Weishi Yin,Hongyu Liu*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文提出基于平均场博弈（MFG）的主动层析成像框架，将未知环境作为空间成本场嵌入运行成本，从种群动力学观测中反演环境。该方法建立了正向MFG模型、观测通道、结构机制和计算恢复路径，数值实验表明在噪声和多通道场景下具有稳定恢复能力，适用于生物运输、血管流动和地下水动力学等由优化和交互种群生成数据的逆问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统走时层析成像假设传播是被动的，环境通过弯曲路径或改变走时影响观测。但许多集体系统并非如此：观测到的到达由策略运动、拥堵和环境成本共同塑造。作者希望建立一种能处理主动传播场景的层析成像框架。

Method: 通过平均场博弈（MFG）建模主动传播：未知环境作为空间成本场进入运行成本，从种群动力学观测中读取数据。提出两阶段反演流程：扩散基初始化 + 完整MFG精化。将正演传播、观测生成和反演统一在PDE约束模型中。

Result: 数值实验表明，该方法在噪声和多通道场景族下具有稳定恢复能力。与传统被动层析成像不同，该框架中动力学、拥堵和环境效应通过时空局部权重内生地耦合，而非外部全局系数。

Conclusion: 该框架为数据由优化和交互种群生成而非被动信号生成的一类逆问题建立了基础性框架，适用于生物运输、血管流动和地下水动力学等场景。

Abstract: Travel-time tomography seeks to recover a hidden environment from external measurements generated by propagation through an anomalous region. Standard formulations treat propagation as passive, so the environment influences observations mainly by bending paths or changing travel times. Many collective systems do not operate in that regime: observed arrivals are shaped by strategic motion, congestion, and environmental costs. We formulate this active setting through mean field games, in which the unknown environment enters the running cost through a spatial cost field and observations are read from the resulting population dynamics. This yields three contributions. First, it places propagation, observation generation, and inversion within one PDE-constrained model. Second, it clarifies why the inverse problem differs structurally from passive tomography: kinetic, congestion, and environmental effects are coupled endogenously and appear through space- and time-dependent local weights rather than externally chosen global coefficients. Third, it introduces a two-stage inversion pipeline that combines diffusion-based initialization with full mean field game refinement, and numerical experiments show stable recovery under noise and across multichannel scene families. Taken together, these ingredients establish a foundational framework for a class of inverse problems in which data are generated by optimizing and interacting populations rather than by passive signals. The framework identifies the forward MFG model, admissible observation channels, structural mechanisms, and computational recovery route needed to study active tomography under collective dynamics. Such problems arise, among other settings, in biological transport, vascular flow, and subsurface groundwater dynamics.

</details>


### [8] [Optimal Harvesting of a Stochastic Logistic Model Driven by One-Sided Tempered Stable Process](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15624)
*Wenmin Deng,Fu Zhang*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文研究了一类由 tempered stable 过程驱动的随机 Logistic 捕捞模型，建立了种群灭绝与持续存在的阈值条件，证明了模型的分布稳定性，推导了最优捕捞努力量与最大可持续产量的显式解，系统分析了白噪声强度与 Lévy 跳跃强度对最优捕捞策略的影响，并重点阐明了 Lévy 测度的稳定性指数与 tempering 参数对最优策略的作用，提出了四种干预策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究随机环境下种群捕捞模型的最优管理策略，特别是考虑具有幂律 Lévy 测度的 tempered stable 过程驱动的 Logistic 模型，以更真实地刻画种群受到的突发性冲击。

Method: 建立随机 Logistic 捕捞模型（由 tempered stable 过程驱动），运用随机分析理论推导种群灭绝与持续存在的阈值条件，证明分布稳定性，并通过优化方法求解最优捕捞努力量与最大可持续产量的显式表达式。

Result: 得到了种群灭绝与持续存在的阈值条件，证明了模型的分布稳定性，推导出最优捕捞努力量和最大可持续产量的显式解，揭示了 Lévy 测度的稳定性指数和 tempering 参数对最优策略的关键影响，并提出了四种靶向干预策略。

Conclusion: Lévy 跳跃的稳定性指数与 tempering 参数深刻影响最优捕捞策略，针对这些结构参数设计的干预策略可为随机扰动下的渔业资源管理提供理论指导。

Abstract: This paper investigates a class of stochastic Logistic harvesting models driven by tempered stable processes, with a one-sided power-law Lévy measure. We establish threshold conditions for population extinction and persistence, prove the distributional stability of the model, and derive explicit solutions for the optimal harvesting effort and the maximum sustainable yield. We systematically analyze the effects of white noise intensity and Lévy jump intensity on the optimal harvesting strategy. In particular, by focusing on the intrinsic structural parameters of the Lévy measure, namely the stability index and the tempering parameter, we elucidate their roles in shaping the optimal strategy and propose four targeted intervention strategies. Numerical simulations are presented to validate the theoretical findings.

</details>


### [9] [Viscosity-Informed Generative Actor-Critic for High-Dimensional Stochastic Optimal Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15668)
*Alen E. Golpashin,Gokul Puthumanaillam,Melkior Ornik,Bruce A. Conway*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种求解有界区域上随机退出时间控制中退化椭圆Hamilton-Jacobi-Bellman方程粘性解的方法，通过将粘性强制转化为以对称正定矩阵为参数的包络生成测试族上的min-max问题，在结构和渐近假设下，值函数逼近的任意一致极限点满足采样测试族上的粘性不等式，实验表明该方法能减少经验粘性违反并提高对扰动动力学的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在处理退化椭圆HJB方程的粘性解时面临数值不稳定和鲁棒性不足的问题，尤其是在随机退出时间控制问题中，需要一种能够有效强制粘性条件并提升对模型扰动鲁棒性的数值方法。

Method: 将粘性强制重新表述为以对称正定矩阵为参数的包络生成测试族上的min-max优化问题；通过结构和渐近假设保证逼近值的任意一致极限点满足采样测试族的粘性不等式。

Result: 数值实验表明该方法能减少经验粘性违反（empirical viscosity violations），并提高在扰动动力学条件下的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 所提出的包络生成测试族min-max框架能有效逼近退化椭圆HJB方程的粘性解，兼具数值精度和对模型不确定性的稳健性，为随机退出时间控制问题提供了可靠的数值求解工具。

Abstract: We introduce a method for approximating viscosity solutions of stationary degenerate elliptic Hamilton--Jacobi--Bellman equations on bounded domains arising in stochastic exit-time control. Viscosity enforcement is formulated as a min--max problem over an envelope-generated test family parameterized by symmetric positive definite matrices. Under structural and asymptotic assumptions, any uniform limit point of the value function approximations satisfies the viscosity inequalities on the sampled test family. Numerical experiments show that the proposed method reduces empirical viscosity violations and improves robustness under perturbed dynamics.

</details>


### [10] [Degree Bounds for Positivstellensätze of general semialgebraic sets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15821)
*Olga Heijmans-Kuryatnikova,Juan C. Vera,Luis F. Zuluaga*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文针对一般紧致半代数集上的多项式极小值逼近问题，改进了Putinar和Schmüdgen的SOS-Positivstellensatz的当前最佳度界，并首次给出了Krivine-Stengle和扩展Handelman的ℝ₊-Positivstellensatz的显式度界。方法基于提升-投影构造，利用Łojasiewicz不等式添加变量表示到集合的距离，将原问题提升到更高维超立方体上，再投影回原空间，统一了多种Positivstellensatz层次结构的度界分析，缩小了超立方体与一般半代数集之间的差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Positivstellensatz层次结构在一般紧致半代数集上的收敛速度（即所需证书多项式的度）缺乏紧的显式界，亟需改进当前已知的最佳度界，并为更多类型的Positivstellensatz提供首次显式度界分析。

Method: 采用提升-投影（lift-and-project）构造：通过添加新变量并利用Łojasiewicz不等式代数化表示集合S的距离，将原问题提升到更高维超立方体上，转化为证明一个相关多项式F在超立方体上的正性；然后通过投影去除添加的变量，将F在超立方体上的非负性证书转化为f在S上的非负性证书。

Result: 改进了Putinar和Schmüdgen的SOS-Positivstellensatz在一般紧致半代数集上的当前最佳度界；首次获得了Krivine-Stengle和扩展Handelman的ℝ₊-Positivstellensatz的显式度界；为线性优化基层次结构在一般紧致半代数集上提供了首个显式度界。

Conclusion: 该统一方法有效缩小了超立方体等简单集与一般半代数集在Positivstellensatz度界分析上的差距，为多种层次结构提供了统一的度界分析框架。

Abstract: Let $p_{\min}$ denote the minimum of a polynomial $p$ over a (general) compact semialgebraic set $S \subseteq \mathbb{R}^n$. A standard way to approximate $p_{\min}$ is via hierarchies built from Positivstellensätze, which certify nonnegativity of polynomials on $S$ using sums of squares or other classes of globally nonnegative polynomials. As the degree of the certificate grows, the values generated by these hierarchies converge asymptotically to $p_{\min}$. A natural question is, then, to determine explicit bounds on the certificate's degree needed to obtain a prescribed $\varepsilon$-approximation to $p_{\min}$, or equivalently certify the positivity of $f:=p - p_{\min} + \varepsilon$ on $S$. We improve the current best degree bounds for Putinar's and Schmüdgen's SOS-Positivstellensatz over $S$. Also, we obtain degree bounds for Krivine--Stengle's and the recently introduced extended-Handelman's $\mathbb{R}_+$-Positivstellensätze over $S$; providing the first explicit degree bounds for linear optimization-based hierarchies over general compact semialgebraic sets. Our approach is based on a lift-and-project construction in which we add new variables to construct an algebraic representation of the distance to the set $S$ using Łojasiewicz's inequality. This lets us lift the problem of certifying the positivity of $f$ on the (complex) set $S$ to the problem of certifying the positivity of a related polynomial $F$ on a higher-dimensional hypercube. By projecting out the added variables, non-negativity certificates for $F$ on the hypercube become non-negativity certificates for $f$ on $S$. Our approach offers a unified methodology to obtain degree bounds for several Positivstellensatz-based hierarchies over general compact sets, narrowing the gap between results for the hypercube (or other simple sets) and more general semialgebraic sets.

</details>


### [11] [Finding directional stationary points of DC programs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15838)
*Hoai An Le Thi,Van Ngai Huynh,Tao Pham Dinh*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文针对非光滑非凸优化问题，提出了一种统一框架来识别DC规划中的方向稳定点。该框架推广了经典DCA算法，适用于两个DC分量都可能非光滑的情形，并在Łojasiewicz不等式条件下证明了序列的全局收敛性，同时引入了随机化变体并证明了其几乎必然收敛。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非光滑非凸优化问题中，计算稳定点的方法在光滑情形下已得到充分研究，但在非光滑情形下算法和理论结果较少。现有DCA算法依赖于特定的DC分解，而方向稳定点是一个不依赖于分解的更强概念，但已有工作仅针对特定非光滑DC规划（第二DC分量为有限个光滑凸函数的最大值）。本文旨在提出一种更通用的统一方法。

Method: 提出了一种统一框架，用于识别非光滑DC规划（两个DC分量均可非光滑）中的方向稳定点。该框架推广了经典DCA算法，适用于第二DC分量为连续族光滑凸函数逐点最大值的情形，更一般地适用于任意连续凸函数。在第二DC分量为有限个C^{1,1}光滑凸函数最大值时，利用Łojasiewicz不等式证明整个序列收敛。此外，引入了随机化（随机）变体并证明其几乎必然收敛。

Result: 建立了强收敛结果：当第二DC分量为有限个C^{1,1}光滑凸函数的最大值时，在Łojasiewicz不等式条件下，算法生成的整个序列收敛；随机化变体几乎必然收敛。这扩展了此前需要全局C^{1,1}光滑性的结果。

Conclusion: 所提出的统一框架同时推广了经典DCA和近期相关方法，为非光滑DC规划的方向稳定点计算提供了更广泛的适用性和更强的收敛保证。

Abstract: We address the problem of computing stationary points for non-smooth, non-convex optimization problems. While this topic is well studied in the smooth setting, fewer algorithmic and theoretical results exist for the non-smooth case. Within Difference-of-Convex functions (DC) programming, the well-known DC Algorithm (DCA) is a standard method for computing critical points, whose definition depends on the chosen DC decomposition. More recently, some works have focused on computing directional stationary points - a stronger notion that does not depend on any particular DC decomposition - for specific non-smooth DC programs, where the second DC component is the pointwise maximum of finitely many smooth convex functions.
  In this contribution, we propose a new and unified approach for identifying directional stationary points of non-smooth DC programs, where both DC components may be non-smooth. Our framework generalizes both the classical DCA and the above recent approaches. It applies when the second DC component is the pointwise maximum of a continuous family of smooth convex functions, and more generally, to any continuous convex function on the whole space. We also establish strong convergence results. Specifically, when the second DC component is the pointwise maximum of finitely many $C^{1,1}$ - smooth convex functions, we prove under the Łojasiewicz inequality that the entire sequence generated by our algorithm converges. This extends previous results requiring global $C^{1,1}$ - smoothness. Finally, we introduce a randomized (stochastic) variant of our method and prove its almost sure convergence, thereby extending our deterministic results to the randomized setting.

</details>


### [12] [Copositive Matrices with Ordered Off-Diagonal Entries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15970)
*Grigoriy Blekherman,Santanu S. Dey,Alex Dunbar,Burak Kocuk*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文研究了可分解为半正定矩阵和非负矩阵之和的共正矩阵，证明了若共正矩阵的非对角元素在行和列上非递减，则存在这样的分解。将该结果应用于标准单纯形上的二次型优化，证明了当目标函数可分离时，该问题的自然松弛是紧的，解决了Dey和Kocuk的一个开放问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究共正矩阵的分解性质，特别是探索在何种条件下共正矩阵可以分解为半正定矩阵与非负矩阵之和，并利用该结果解决二次型优化中的松弛紧性问题。

Method: 通过理论分析，证明共正矩阵在非对角元素按行和列非递减的条件下具有上述分解性质；然后将该结果应用于标准单纯形上的二次型优化问题，推导出可分离目标函数情形下自然松弛的紧性。

Result: 证明了若共正矩阵的非对角元素在行和列上非递减，则存在半正定矩阵与非负矩阵的分解；并以此证明了可分离目标函数下二次型优化问题的自然松弛是紧的。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了共正矩阵的一类重要分解条件，并成功应用于优化理论，解决了Dey和Kocuk提出的开放问题，为相关领域的进一步研究提供了理论工具。

Abstract: We study copositive matrices which admit a decomposition into a sum of a positive semidefinite matrix and a matrix with nonnegative entries. Our main result shows that if the off-diagonal entries of a copositive matrix are nondecreasing in rows and in columns, then it admits such a decomposition. We apply this result to study optimization of quadratic forms over the standard simplex. As a corollary, we obtain that a natural relaxation of this problem is tight when the objective function is separable, resolving an open question of Dey and Kocuk.

</details>


### [13] [Singular control with state-dependent costs for Lévy processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15993)
*Mordecki Ernesto,Muler Nora,Oliú Facundo*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 最小化由运行成本和控制成本（依赖当前状态）组成的成本泛函，并寻找最优反射屏障策略。

Method: 建立HJB型验证定理；通过概率工具将控制问题与最优停时问题建立联系，证明最优反射阈值等于辅助问题的最优停时边界。

Result: 证明了最优反射阈值与辅助最优停时问题的停时边界一致，并在若干相关案例中得到显式或半显式解。

Conclusion: 该连接提供了概率论视角下的最优策略刻画，并通过污染治理等应用实例验证了理论结果的有效性。

Abstract: We study a discounted singular stochastic control problem driven by a general Lévy process, where the objective is to minimize a cost functional composed of a running cost and a control cost that depends on the current state of the process. We first establish a Hamilton Jacobi Bellman (HJB)-type verification theorem providing sufficient conditions under which a reflecting barrier strategy is optimal and characterizing the value function. Our main contribution is to connect this control problem with an associated optimal stopping problem: we prove that the optimal reflection threshold coincides with the optimal stopping boundary of the auxiliary problem. This connection allows us to characterize the optimal strategy through probabilistic tools and leads to explicit or semi-explicit solutions in several relevant cases. We illustrate the results with several examples, including an application to pollution abatement.

### [14] [GoldNash: A Goldfarb-Idnani Variant for Strongly Monotone Linear-Quadratic Games](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16002)
*Alberto Bemporad*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文提出了GoldNash算法，是Goldfarb-Idnani对偶积极集方法在变分广义纳什均衡计算中的变体，适用于强单调N人博弈，具有凸二次成本和共享仿射不等式与等式约束。该方法在保持原算法性质的同时，可处理非对称伪梯度矩阵，数值实验表明其优于现有算法，并能高效计算博弈论线性模型预测控制律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出GoldNash算法，即Goldfarb-Idnani对偶积极集方法的一个变体。该方法保持了原算法的核心性质，但能处理博弈联合KKT系统中可能出现的非对称伪梯度矩阵，从而适用于具有凸二次成本和共享仿射约束的强单调N人博弈。

Result: 数值结果表明，GoldNash方法在大多数情况下优于现有最先进算法，并且能够非常高效地计算博弈论线性模型预测控制律。

Conclusion: GoldNash方法有效扩展了Goldfarb-Idnani方法的应用范围至非合作博弈领域，提供了一种高效的变分广义纳什均衡计算工具。该算法的Python实现已在开源NashOpt库中公开。

Abstract: We present a simple variant of the Goldfarb-Idnani (GI) dual active-set method for computing variational generalized Nash equilibria of strongly monotone N-player games with convex quadratic costs and shared affine inequality and equality constraints. We prove that the original properties of the algorithm are maintained in spite of having a possibly non-symmetric pseudogradient matrix in the joint KKT system of the game. Our numerical results show that the method, which we call GoldNash, most often outperforms alternative state-of-the-art algorithms and enables very efficient computations of game-theoretic linear model predictive control laws. A Python implementation of the algorithm is available in the open-source NashOpt library.

### [15] [A New Constraint Qualification for Mixed Constrained Optimal Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16021)
*Rodrigo B. Moreira,Valeriano A. de Oliveira*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文针对混合约束最优控制问题中提出的渐近弱极大值原理，设计了一种新的约束规范，证明在该规范下渐近弱极大值原理可推出经典弱极大值原理，且在光滑情形下该约束规范是最弱的能具备此性质的约束规范，同时给出了该约束规范的充分判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 渐近弱极大值原理虽不依赖混合约束的正则性条件且可作为数值方法的终止准则，但在某些情况下其鲁棒性不足，可能被非极值过程满足，因此需要设计一种约束规范来加强其与经典最优性条件之间的联系。

Method: 提出一种新的约束规范，通过理论分析证明其能够使渐近弱极大值原理蕴含经典弱极大值原理，并在光滑框架下通过极值分析证明该约束规范是最弱的具有此性质的规范，同时给出确保该规范成立的充分条件。

Result: 所提出的约束规范使得渐近弱极大值原理可推出经典弱极大值原理；在光滑设定下，该约束规范是最弱且能实现此推导的约束规范；此外给出了验证该约束规范有效性的充分判据。

Conclusion: 该研究为渐近弱极大值原理的理论完善提供了关键的约束规范条件，加强了其为数理最优性条件的适用性和严谨性。

Abstract: In recent developments, a novel set of necessary optimality conditions for mixed constrained optimal control problems, termed the asymptotic weak maximum principle, has been formulated. These novel conditions deviate from the classical ones by virtue of their sequential nature and the fact that they are satisfied regardless of the regularity conditions imposed on the mixed constraints. Furthermore, due to their asymptotic behaviour, these conditions serve as a precise tool for use as stopping criteria in numerical methods of solution. However, it should be noted that, in certain instances, these conditions may not be sufficiently robust to fully characterize optimal solutions, as they can be satisfied by processes that are not extremals. The present study proposes a novel constraint qualification, meticulously developed to address these asymptotic optimality conditions. It is demonstrated that the asymptotic weak maximum principle implies the classical weak maximum principle when the newly proposed constraint qualification is verified. It is further demonstrated that, in the smooth setting, this constraint qualification is the weakest one that possesses such a property. Additionally, this study present sufficient criteria for the validity of the newly proposed constraint qualification.

</details>


### [16] [Stochastic Compositional Optimization via Hybrid Momentum Frank--Wolfe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15350)
*El Mahdi Chayti*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 提出混合动量随机Frank-Wolfe算法，去除了组合优化中外函数F必须光滑的假设，在非凸Lipschitz外函数设置下达到了O(K^{-1/4})的收敛率，并支持重尾噪声。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有随机组合优化方法均假设外函数F连续可微，这排除了许多实际应用（如鲁棒最大损失、条件风险价值、范数正则化器），因此需要一种不依赖F光滑性的算法。

Method: 结合动量Jacobian追踪器和Taylor校正函数追踪器，将完整的随机线性化（而非单个梯度）输入广义线性最小化 oracle，形成混合动量随机Frank-Wolfe算法。

Result: 对L_F-Lipschitz外函数的非凸目标，在广义Frank-Wolfe间隙上达到O(K^{-1/4})收敛率，匹配无投影单样本随机方法在期望光滑性下的最优复杂度；分析还扩展到具有有界r阶矩（r∈(1,2]）的重尾噪声，并在噪声消失时恢复确定性的收敛速率。

Conclusion: 该工作首次在组合优化中去除了外函数光滑性要求，同时保持了最优收敛率和对重尾噪声的鲁棒性。

Abstract: Stochastic compositional optimization minimizes objectives of the form $\min_{\bm{x} \in \mathcal{X}} F(\bm{f}(\bm{x}), \bm{x})$, where $\bm{f}$ is accessible only through noisy stochastic queries. Existing methods for this problem assume that the outer function $F$ is continuously differentiable, which excludes many practically important applications such as robust max-of-losses, Conditional Value-at-Risk, and norm regularizers. We propose the Hybrid Momentum Stochastic Frank--Wolfe algorithm, which drops the smoothness assumption on $F$. By combining a momentum-based Jacobian tracker with a Taylor-corrected function tracker, the algorithm feeds an entire stochastic linearization -- rather than a single gradient -- into a generalized linear minimization oracle. We establish an $\mathcal{O}(K^{-1/4})$ convergence rate in the generalized Frank--Wolfe gap for non-convex objectives with $L_F$-Lipschitz outer functions, matching the optimal complexity for projection-free single-sample stochastic methods under expected smoothness. The analysis extends to heavy-tailed noise oracles with bounded $r$-th moments for $r \in (1, 2]$ and recovers the deterministic rates of Vladarean et al (2023) as the noise vanishes.

</details>

### [17] [Testing properties of trees in graphical models with covariance queries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15996)
*Sofiya Burova,Francisco Calvillo,Gábor Lugosi,Piotr Zwiernik*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文研究高维图模型中树结构图的全局属性测试问题，采用协方差查询模型，设计出使用次二次查询次数的随机化测试程序，用于测试叶子数、最大度、典型距离和直径等关键属性，并给出了显式的查询复杂度界限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高维图模型中，完全重建树结构代价高昂，而许多应用场景仅需测试某些全局结构属性（如树是稀疏还是密集、直径是大还是小等），因此有动机设计高效的属性测试算法来替代完整的图重建。

Method: 采用Lugosi等人提出的协方差查询模型，针对树结构图设计随机化测试算法。利用协方差矩阵中蕴含的图结构信息，通过次二次数量的查询来推断全局属性，并对每个属性给出依赖于阈值和容错参数的查询复杂度界限。

Result: 给出了针对叶子数、最大度、典型距离、直径等树结构全局属性的显式查询复杂度上界，证明在次二次查询次数下即可有效测试这些属性。

Conclusion: 揭示了在高维图模型中，虽然完全重建树结构成本较高，但利用协方差查询可以高效测试树的多种全局结构属性，为高维图模型的属性测试提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We consider the problem of testing properties of graphs underlying high-dimensional graphical models. We adopt the model of covariance queries introduced by Lugosi, Truszkowski, Velona, and Zwiernik (2021). We study the case when the underlying graph is a tree. The main results of the paper show that, while reconstructing the entire tree may be costly, certain global structural properties can be tested efficiently. In particular, we design randomized tests for global structural properties that use a sub-quadratic number of queries. We develop testing procedures for several fundamental properties, including the number of leaves, the maximum degree, the typical distance, and the diameter of the tree. ### [18] [Explainable AI Isn't Enough! Rethinking Algorithmic Contestability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16041)
*Timo Freiesleben,Kristof Meding,Gunnar König*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文提出了算法可争议性（algorithmic contestability）的形式化定义，将其与算法追索（algorithmic recourse）区分开来，并识别了三种可以推翻算法决策的证据类型：预测多样性、错误特征值和被忽略的压倒性证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有XAI研究主要关注算法追索（帮助个体改变特征以获得理想结果），但忽视了算法可争议性（帮助个体审查和纠正错误决策）这一同等重要的伦理和法律问题，缺乏清晰的形式化定义和系统化操作框架。

Method: 通过对比分析定义可争议性与追索的本质区别，论证传统XAI解释方法（反事实、LIME、Anchors）的局限性，进而识别三种可推翻决策的证据类型，并结合欧盟法律框架进行分析。

Result: 标准XAI解释即使结合人类直觉（连续性或单调性），也只能揭示个体邻域内的错误，但不足以推翻当前决策。识别出三种可证伪决策的证据：预测多样性、错误特征值、被忽略的压倒性证据。

Conclusion: 算法可争议性是算法追索的自然补充，个体已有法律权利主张上述三类证据，为构建更公平的算法问责机制提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Machine learning systems increasingly make life-changing decisions about individuals, such as loan approvals, hiring, and cheating detection, raising a pressing question: how can individuals respond to negative decisions made by these opaque systems? While explainable artificial intelligence (XAI) has largely focused on algorithmic recourse -- helping individuals change their features to obtain a desired outcome -- the parallel problem of algorithmic contestability -- helping individuals review and correct erroneous algorithmic decisions -- has received far less attention, despite its central ethical and legal importance. We trace this neglect to the absence of clear formal definitions and a systematic operationalization of contestability as an algorithmic problem. To address it, we propose an operational definition of contestability as a natural complement to recourse: contestability starts from the presumption that a decision may be incorrect and focuses on identifying evidence to challenge and potentially overturn it, whereas recourse assumes the decision is valid and instead provides pathways for changing it. We show that standard XAI explanations, such as counterfactuals, LIME, or Anchors, even when combined with human intuitions about decision continuity or monotonicity, reveal only errors in the neighborhood of the individual, but provide insufficient grounds for overturning the decision at hand. Going thus beyond traditional XAI, we identify three types of evidence warranting reversal according to the decision maker's own ethical standards: predictive multiplicity, incorrect feature values, and neglected overruling evidence. We argue that these render decisions normatively indefensible and thus successfully contestable. Finally, we analyze how existing EU legislation connects to our framework and argue that individuals already hold some legal rights to these forms of evidence.

### [19] [A numerical study into neural network surrogate model performance for uncertainty propagation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16078)
*Noah Wade,Kirubel Teferra*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文系统评估了神经网络代理模型在随机边界值问题中捕获完整解分布（尤其是尾部极端样本）的能力。以高度随机源项的热传导方程为基准，对比了全连接网络和DeepONet架构在数据驱动和物理信息损失函数下的表现。结果表明极端样本的预测误差比平均场误差大一个数量级，根本原因是网络需要对训练数据范围之外的输入进行外推。研究提出了识别这些外推样本的方法，并发现使用弱形式残差损失训练的全连接网络在处理外推输入时表现最佳。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究主要关注神经网络代理模型在确定性样本或均场解上的表现，忽视了其在分布尾部（极端样本）的预测能力。鉴于随机问题中尾部行为对风险评估和可靠性分析至关重要，需要系统评估代理模型在整个概率空间上的性能。

Method: 以热传导方程（含高度随机源项）为基准问题，对比经典全连接前馈网络和Deep Operator Network两种架构，分别采用数据驱动损失函数和物理信息损失函数（弱形式残差损失）进行训练，系统评估模型在整个概率空间及尾部的预测表现。

Result: 极端样本的预测误差比平均场误差大一个数量级；大误差源于网络需对训练数据范围外的输入进行外推；使用弱形式残差损失训练的全连接网络在处理外推输入时预测精度最高。

Abstract: Neural network surrogate models have emerged as a promising approach to model solution fields for a wide variety of boundary value problems encountered in physical modeling. Stochastic problems represent an area of particularly high interest because of the potential to significantly reduce the repeated evaluation of expensive forward models via traditional numerical solvers when conducting parametric analysis. However, many studies found in the literature primarily focus on the ability of neural network surrogate models to represent deterministic samples or mean field solutions and largely overlook surrogate model performance at the tails of the distribution. The present study examines in detail the ability of neural network surrogate models to capture the full distribution of solution fields over the entire probability space, while emphasis is placed at the tails of the distribution. Serving as a canonical problem is the heat conduction equation with a highly stochastic source term, inducing extremely large variation in the thermal solution field. Comparisons are made between a classic feed-forward fully connected network and a Deep Operator Network architecture, using both data-driven and physics-informed loss functions. Results show that the worst-case prediction errors are an order of magnitude larger than the mean field error, highlighting the importance of the outlier samples. The large errors associated with extreme samples result from the networks having to extrapolate beyond the bounds of the training data. A method for identifying these samples is presented along with a discussion of potential approaches to account of their errors. Among the models considered, the fully connected neural network trained using a weak form residual loss performs best in handling these extrapolated inputs, achieving the highest prediction accuracy for the numerically produced datasets.

Abstract: We develop a skew-adaptive extension of split conformal prediction for regression. The method starts from an asymmetric interval family centered at a point prediction and uses the gauge approach to deduce the conformity score induced by this family. The inverse hyperbolic sine transform of signed scaled residuals provides the training target for an additional predictive model, whose role is to learn how predictive uncertainty should tilt across the feature space. The resulting procedure preserves the finite-sample marginal validity of split conformal prediction under exchangeability, while producing intervals that adapt to both local scale and local skewness. We also develop a calibration-sample-based estimator for comparing the expected relative future width of the skew-adaptive and classical scaled-score intervals. Experiments on a variety of datasets indicate gains in prediction interval efficiency over the scaled-score construction and conformalized quantile regression, and show that the proposed estimator closely matches the corresponding average width ratio observed on the test sample.

We introduce QSurv, a scalable deep learning framework that enables nonparametric continuous-time modeling without relying on time discretization or restrictive distributional assumptions. We propose a training objective based on Gauss-Legendre numerical quadrature, which approximates the cumulative hazard with high-order accuracy while facilitating efficient end-to-end training via standard backpropagation. Furthermore, to effectively capture non-stationary hazard dynamics in complex architectures, we introduce time-conditioned low-rank adaptation, a mechanism that conditions general neural backbones on time by dynamically modulating weights via low-rank updates. We provide theoretical analysis establishing approximation error bounds for cumulative-hazard evaluation. Comprehensive experiments across synthetic benchmarks, large-scale real-world tabular datasets, and high-dimensional medical imaging tasks demonstrate that QSurv achieves competitive predictive performance with advantages in instantaneous hazard function estimation, enabling more interpretable characterization of time-varying risk patterns.

### [22] [Harnessing Unimodality in Semiparametric Contextual Pricing via Oracle Price Map Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15411)

Method: 提出ORBIT策略，包括：（1）标量引导指数（pilot index）作为输入；（2）在每个活跃区间（bin）内定位基准价格；（3）通过置信域内的带状凸优化（bandit convex optimization）学习Oracle价格映射的局部多项式近似。对于线性效用模型，采用自适应椭圆探索方案在线构造标量引导，无需对上下文分布做假设。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了半参数标量指数模型下Oracle价格映射的平滑性传递机制（从尾函数β-光滑到映射(β-1)-光滑），并通过ORBIT策略实现了近乎最优的后悔界。标量引导接口具有良好的模块化扩展性，可适用于多种效用模型。

Abstract: We study contextual dynamic pricing in a semiparametric scalar-index valuation model where the latent value is $v_t=μ_\ast(\mathsf c_t)+ξ_t$, with an unknown utility map $μ_\ast$ and an unknown additive noise distribution. The key decision object is the one-dimensional oracle price map $u\mapsto p^\ast(u)$ induced by the scalar index $u=μ_\ast(\mathsf c)$ and the noise tail. Under the $β$-Hölder smoothness of the tail function for $β\geq 2$ and a revenue-geometry condition that gives a unique, stable, interior maximizer, this oracle map is itself $(β-1)$-smooth. We exploit such structure through $\mathsf{ORBIT}$, a modular coarse-to-fine policy that takes a scalar pilot index as input, localizes a benchmark price in each active bin, and learns a local polynomial approximation of the oracle map inside a trust region via bandit convex optimization. For the baseline linear utility model $μ_\ast(\mathsf c)=\mathsf c^\topθ_\ast$, an adaptive elliptical exploration scheme constructs the required scalar pilot online without distributional assumptions on the contexts. The resulting policy achieves regret $\widetilde{O}\big(T^{\frac{2β-1}{4β-3}}+\sqrt{dT}\big)$. For fixed $d$, we establish a matching lower bound in the horizon dependence, unveiling that the nonparametric oracle-map learning term is minimax sharp. The same scalar-pilot interface also yields extensions to sparse high-dimensional linear utility and nonparametric Hölder utility.

Abstract: Concept Activation Vectors (CAVs) are a fundamental tool for concept-based explainability in deep learning, yet their practical utility is limited by statistical instability. We analyze the stochastic nature of CAVs and the Testing with CAVs (TCAV) method, deriving the distributions of major CAV classes including PatternCAV, FastCAV, and ridge regression-based CAVs. We then identify a fundamental flaw in the standard TCAV score: its reliance on a discontinuous indicator function induces non-decaying variance in critical regimes. To address this, we introduce $α$-TCAV, a generalized framework that replaces the indicator with a parameterized smooth function, yielding a unified probabilistic formulation that subsumes both TCAV and Multi-TCAV. We characterize the induced distributions of sensitivity scores and different TCAV variants, showing that established state-of-the-art choices lack theoretical justification. Finally, our analysis yields practical recommendations that challenge established routines: most notably, allocating the full sampling budget to a single CAV rather than splitting it across several.

Abstract: This paper investigates the critical role of eigenalignments between the kernel matrix and learning targets in achieving robust generalization in learning problems. We establish a direct connection between generalization performance in kernel methods and the estimation of eigenvectors and eigenvalues of matrices, offering a more intuitive understanding compared to prior work with minimal assumptions. We also show that, since the prediction task in KRR is essentially the weighted sum of eigenvectors/singular vectors, by analyzing how much error can be caused by perturbations to the kernel matrix, we can then derive a bound on this generalization error using the estimation stability of matrix eigenvalues and eigenvectors. Compared with previous work, our analysis concentrates on finite-sample settings and on the generalization error arising from having a suboptimal finite training set. Our findings reveal that in kernel methods, as long as the kernel is of high rank, the near-zero reconstruction error can be trivially obtained, implying that the reconstruction error will have limited predictive power for generalization. Finally, we establish a generalization bound from an eigenvalues/eigenvectors estimation perspective, showing that strong generalization requires increasing eigenvector alignment, eigenvalue magnitude, or gaps between consecutive eigenvalues.

### [25] [MaxSketch: Robust Distinct Counting in Streams via Random Projections](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15571)
*Nikos Tsikouras,Constantine Caramanis,Christos Tzamos*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文提出MaxSketch，一种利用随机高斯投影的max-linear草图，用于在高维噪声数据流中估计不同对象的数量。在潜在对象具有几何结构（常见于学习表示）的假设下，仅需Õ(log n/ε²)个随机投影即可实现(1+ε)因子内的准确估计，显著优于一般度量空间Ω̃(√n)的最坏情况下界。实验验证了其在图像流上的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典流式不同元素计数方法（如HyperLogLog）假设重复元素完全一致，但在现代高维噪声场景下（如不同图像中同一人的像素级差异），相同对象仅近似相似，导致哈希一致性失效。现有针对一般度量空间的鲁棒算法在最坏情况下需要Ω̃(√n)内存，作者希望探讨是否能利用学习表示中常见的几何结构来实现更高效的计数。

Method: 提出MaxSketch方法，基于随机高斯投影构建max-linear草图：对每个数据点，通过多个随机高斯向量进行线性投影并取最大值（max）作为草图值。在潜在对象服从某个未知度量结构（如低维流形或聚类结构）的假设下，利用几何性质证明少量投影即可实现高精度估计。

Result: 理论证明：在几何结构假设下，Õ(log n/ε²)个随机投影（即Õ(log n/ε²)内存）即可在(1+ε)因子内恢复真实不同对象计数。对比一般度量空间下界Ω̃(√n)，实现了指数级改进。实验表明MaxSketch在图像流上准确估计不同对象数量，且能泛化到训练分布之外的场景。

Conclusion: 本文桥接了经典流式算法与现代表示学习，揭示了利用几何结构可以从根本上降低不同元素计数的复杂度。MaxSketch为处理高维噪声数据流中的去重计数提供了实用的解决方案。

Abstract: Estimating the number of distinct elements in a data stream is well understood when repeated elements are identical. In modern settings, however, observations are high-dimensional and noisy, so repeated instances of the same object are only approximately similar -- for example, different images of the same individual may vary significantly at the pixel level. Classical sketches such as HyperLogLog rely on consistent hash values for identical elements and break down in this regime. Recent work on robust distinct counting in general metric spaces achieves $\widetildeΘ(\sqrt{n})$ memory, which is tight in the worst case. We show that substantially improved memory guarantees are possible under geometric structure common in learned representations. We introduce MaxSketch, a simple max-linear sketch built from random Gaussian projections, and prove that it succeeds in estimating the number of distinct latent objects. Concretely, we show that under this assumption $m = \widetilde{O} (\log n / \varepsilon^2)$ random projections (and hence $\widetilde{O} (\log n/\varepsilon^2)$ memory) suffice to recover the true distinct count within a $(1+\varepsilon)$ factor. Experiments on image streams confirm that MaxSketch accurately estimates distinct counts and generalizes beyond the training regime. Our results bridge classical streaming algorithms and modern representation learning, showing how geometric structure can fundamentally reduce the complexity of distinct counting.

</details>


### [26] [Pessimistic Risk-Aware Policy Learning in Contextual Bandits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15620)
*Yilong Wan,Yuqiang Li,Xianyi Wu*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文研究风险感知的离线策略学习，提出统一分布框架优化Lipschitz连续风险泛函，推导出$\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(1/\sqrt{n})$率的数据依赖次优性界，证明该率在极小极大意义下最优且与风险中性情况匹配。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高风险场景中，需要从离线日志数据中学习在一般风险准则下最优的决策规则，而现有离线情境赌博机文献要么关注期望回报准则，要么将风险考量局限于策略评估而非优化。

Method: 提出统一分布框架用于优化Lipschitz连续风险泛函（涵盖均值-方差、熵风险、条件风险价值等）；开发基于重要性采样的分布估计量的新型经验集中不等式；推导出不依赖统一重叠假设的数据依赖次优性界。

Result: 获得$\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(1/\sqrt{n})$率的次优性界，该率是极小极大最优的，且与风险中性离线策略优化相匹配。

Conclusion: 优化一般Lipschitz风险准则相对于期望回报准则不会产生额外的统计代价。

Abstract: We study risk-aware offline policy learning, aiming to learn a decision rule from logged data that is optimal under general risk criteria. This problem is crucial in high-stakes domains where online interaction is infeasible and adverse outcomes must be carefully controlled. However, existing literature on offline contextual bandits either centers on expected-reward criteria or restricts risk considerations to policy evaluation instead of optimization. In this work, we propose a unified distributional framework for optimizing Lipschitz-continuous risk functionals, a broad class of risk measures encompassing mean-variance, entropic risk, and conditional value-at-risk, among others. By developing novel empirical concentration inequalities for importance sampling-based distributional estimators, our analysis derives data-dependent suboptimality bounds with an $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(1/\sqrt{n})$ rate, without relying on restrictive uniform overlap assumptions. This rate is minimax optimal and matches that of risk-neutral offline policy optimization, indicating that optimizing general Lipschitz risk criteria incurs no additional statistical cost relative to the expected-reward.

</details>


### [27] [Unsupervised Domain Shift Detection with Interpretable Subspace Attribution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15920)
*Sebastian Springer,Alessandro Laio*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种检测高维数据中域偏移（分布差异）的工具，能够定位异常密度区域、归因于特定特征子空间，并通过提取无残留差异的子集来补偿偏移。在20维合成基准和782维心电图数据上验证了有效性，揭示了设备引起的隐藏偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数据集中概率分布的细微差异（域偏移）可能导致下游模型性能下降或引入偏差，现有方法缺乏对偏移的可解释定位和补偿手段。

Method: 1) 设计检测高维特征空间中局部密度异常的算法；2) 识别异常最显著的特征子空间，实现可解释的偏移归因；3) 提出从两个无标签数据集中提取无残留分布差异子集的补偿协议。

Result: 在20维合成基准上准确恢复了宽泛和局部偏移及其支持特征子空间；在782维心电图数据中成功检测到设备引起的偏移，提取了富含失衡设备成分的代表性子集，并识别出与采集对比相关的ECG特征。

Conclusion: 密度偏移检测与子空间归因为在下游建模前发现隐藏的队列偏差提供了实用框架。

Abstract: We developed a tool for detecting domain shifts, namely subtle differences in the probability distributions of datasets. We identify these shifts using an algorithm designed to detect localised density anomalies in high-dimensional feature spaces. If an anomaly is present, we then identify the feature subspace in which the anomaly is most pronounced. This allows us to trace the domain shift to a small set of features, making the shift interpretable. Moreover, we provide a protocol for compensating domain shifts by extracting, from two unlabelled datasets, subsets of samples with no detectable residual distributional difference. We validate the framework on controlled 20-dimensional benchmarks with known ground truth, recovering both broad and localized shifts together with their supporting feature subspaces. We then apply it to healthy electrocardiogram (ECG) recordings represented by 782 features. In age- and sex-matched cohort comparisons differing in measurement-device composition, the method detects device-induced shifts, extracts representative subsets enriched in the imbalanced device components, and identifies ECG features associated with the acquisition contrast. These results suggest that density-shift detection and subspace attribution provide a practical framework for uncovering hidden cohort biases before downstream modelling.

</details>

### [28] [DeepSlide: From Artifacts to Presentation Delivery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15202)
*Ming Yang,Zhiwei Zhang,Jiahang Li,Haoseng Liu,Yuzheng Cai,Weiguo Zheng*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: DeepSlide是一个人类参与的多智能体系统，专注于优化演示文稿的整个准备和交付过程（包括叙事规划、时间预算、脚本生成和排练支持），而不仅仅是生成视觉上合理的幻灯片。在20个领域和不同受众中，它在保持静态幻灯片质量的同时，显著提升了叙事流畅度、节奏精确性和幻灯片-脚本协同等交付指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI幻灯片生成器大多只优化视觉外观（制品质量），而忽视了交付过程（节奏、叙事、演讲准备），导致生成的幻灯片在实际演讲中效果不佳。

Method: DeepSlide采用人机协作的多智能体系统架构，包含：(i) 可控逻辑链规划器（带节点时间预算）、(ii) 轻量级内容树检索器（用于证据接地）、(iii) 马尔科夫式序列渲染（带样式继承）、(iv) 沙盒执行与最小化修复（确保可渲染性）。同时引入双记分板基准，分离评估静态制品质量和动态交付表现。

Result: 在20个领域和多样化受众画像中，DeepSlide在静态制品质量上与强基线相当，但在交付指标上持续取得更大增益，包括叙事流畅度、节奏精确性、幻灯片-脚本协同以及更清晰的注意力引导。

Conclusion: 通过同时优化制品质量和交付过程，DeepSlide证明了在学术演讲场景中，关注完整演示流程（而不仅是最终视觉产物）能够更有效地提升整体沟通效果。

Abstract: Presentations are a primary medium for scholarly communication, yet most AI slide generators optimize the artifact (a visually plausible deck) while under-optimizing the delivery process (pacing, narrative, and presentation preparation). We present DeepSlide, a human-in-the-loop multi-agent system that supports preparing the full presentation process, from requirement elicitation and time-budgeted narrative planning, to evidence-grounded slide--script generation, attention augmentation, and rehearsal support. DeepSlide integrates (i) a controllable logical-chain planner with per-node time budgets, (ii) a lightweight content-tree retriever for grounding, (iii) Markov-style sequential rendering with style inheritance, and (iv) sandboxed execution with minimal repair to ensure renderability. We further introduce a dual-scoreboard benchmark that cleanly separates static artifact quality from dynamic delivery excellence. Across 20 domains and diverse audience profiles, DeepSlide matches strong baselines on artifact quality while consistently achieving larger gains on delivery metrics, improving narrative flow, pacing precision, and slide--script synergy with clearer attention guidance.

### [29] [SDOF: Taming the Alignment Tax in Multi-Agent Orchestration with State-Constrained Dispatch](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15204)
*Zhantao Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: SDOF是一个将多智能体编排转化为约束状态机的框架，通过在线RLHF意图路由器和状态感知调度器实现可审计的执行控制。在基于Beisen iTalent平台的招聘系统中，其7B模型在FSM约束对抗路由基准上达到80.9%的联合准确率（GPT-4o为48.9%），端到端任务完成率86.5%，并阻止了所有22个注入和非法HR操作。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多智能体编排框架（如LangChain、LangGraph、CrewAI）通过图结构流水线路由任务，但未能强制执行真实业务流程中的阶段约束，缺乏对业务状态流转的合规性保障。

Method: SDOF将多智能体执行建模为受约束的状态机，包含两层防御：1) 基于在线RLHF的专用意图路由器（通过生成式奖励建模GRPO训练）；2) 状态感知调度器，包括GoalStage有限自动机检查和前置/后置条件SkillRegistry验证，实现可审计的执行控制。

Result: 在招聘系统中，185个专家策划场景触发1671个实时API调用。GSPO对齐的7B意图路由器在FSM约束对抗路由基准上联合准确率80.9%（零样本GPT-4o为48.9%）。端到端任务完成率86.5%（95%置信区间80.8-90.7），阻止所有22个注入和非法HR操作。消息级审计精度100%、召回88%，专家一致性kappa=0.94。

Conclusion: SDOF通过引入有限状态机约束有效增强了多智能体系统的执行安全性和业务合规性，在真实企业场景中显著优于现有方法。未来将发布扩展的多种子训练对比和更深层工作流评估。

Abstract: Multi-agent orchestration frameworks such as LangChain, LangGraph, and CrewAI route tasks through graph-based pipelines but do not enforce the stage constraints that govern real business processes. We present SDOF, a framework that treats multi-agent execution as a constrained state machine. SDOF operates through two primary defensive layers, implemented by three components: (1) an Online-RLHF Specialized Intent Router trained via Generative Reward Modeling (GRPO) and (2) a StateAwareDispatcher with GoalStage finite-automaton checks and precondition/postcondition SkillRegistry validation for auditable execution control. On a recruitment system backed by the Beisen iTalent platform (6000+ enterprises), 185 expert-curated scenarios trigger 1671 live API calls. Our GSPO-aligned 7B Intent Router achieves higher joint accuracy than zero-shot GPT-4o on this FSM-constrained adversarial routing benchmark (80.9% versus 48.9%). In end-to-end execution, SDOF reaches 86.5% task completion (95% confidence interval 80.8 to 90.7) and blocks all 22 operations in the injection, illegal HR subset. Under a broader message-level blocking audit, SDOF attains precision 100% and recall 88%, expert agreement kappa=0.94. A separate evaluation on 960 SGD-derived dialogues spanning 8 service domains surfaces 201 stage-order conflicts under our FSM mapping, 41 of which arise in the normal split. This arXiv version reports the current validated scope; extended multi-seed training comparisons and deeper workflow evaluations will be released in a subsequent update.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有ToM评估多采用故事阅读、第三人称选择题等静态方式，忽视了人机交互中第一人称、动态、开放式的特点，无法直接衡量ToM改进技术对人机交互的实际效益。

Method: 1）提出交互式ToM评估新范式，包含视角转变（第三人称→第一人称）和度量转变（静态选择题→动态交互指标）；2）对四种代表性ToM增强技术进行系统研究，使用四个真实世界数据集和一项用户研究，覆盖目标导向任务（编程、数学）和体验导向任务（咨询）。

Conclusion: 交互式评估对于开发具有社会感知能力的下一代LLM至关重要，是实现人机共生的必要条件。

Abstract: Improving the Theory of Mind (ToM) capability of Large Language Models (LLMs) is crucial for effective social interactions between these AI models and humans. However, the existing benchmarks often measure ToM capability improvement through story-reading, multiple-choice questions from a third-person perspective, while ignoring the first-person, dynamic, and open-ended nature of human-AI (HAI) interactions. To directly examine how ToM improvement techniques benefit HAI interactions, we first proposed the new paradigm of interactive ToM evaluation with both perspective and metric shifts. Next, following the paradigm, we conducted a systematic study of four representative ToM enhancement techniques using both four real-world datasets and a user study, covering both goal-oriented tasks (e.g., coding, math) and experience-oriented tasks (e.g., counseling). Our findings reveal that improvements on static benchmarks do not always translate to better performance in dynamic HAI interactions. This paper offers critical insights into ToM evaluation, showing the necessity of interaction-based assessments in developing next-generation, socially aware LLMs for HAI symbiosis.

### [31] [SkillSmith: Compiling Agent Skills into Boundary-Guided Runtime Interfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15215)
*Duling Xu,Zheng Chen,Zaifeng Pan,Jiawei Guan,Dong Dong,Jialin Li,Bangzheng Pu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: SkillSmith 提出了一种边界优先的编译-运行时框架，将技能包离线编译为最小可执行接口，通过提取细粒度操作边界，使智能体在运行时仅动态访问和执行相关组件，从而减少无关上下文注入和重复推理开销。在 SkillsBench 基准测试中，相比使用原始技能，解决了阶段 Token 使用量减少 57.44%，思考迭代减少 42.99%，求解时间减少 50.57%，成本降低 57.44%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于 LLM 的智能体系统中，技能通常在运行时作为上下文指导注入推理循环，该范式存在两大冗余来源：无关上下文注入和重复的技能特定推理与规划，导致效率低下和成本高昂。

Method: 提出 SkillSmith 框架，采用边界优先的编译-运行时架构：离线阶段将技能包编译为最小可执行接口并提取细粒度操作边界；运行时阶段智能体仅动态访问和执行相关组件，避免不必要的上下文注入和重复推理开销。编译产物可在不同模型间复用。

Result: 在 SkillsBench 基准上，相比原始技能方案，解决了阶段 Token 使用量减少 57.44%，思考迭代次数减少 42.99%，求解时间减少 50.57%（加速 2.02 倍），Token 比例货币成本降低 57.44%。强模型编译的产物可被小模型复用，在原始技能解释失败时提升任务准确率。

Conclusion: SkillSmith 通过边界优先的编译-运行时框架有效解决了现有 LLM 智能体系统中技能冗余注入和重复推理的问题，大幅降低了计算开销和成本，且编译产物具有良好的跨模型复用性。

Abstract: Recently, skills have been widely adopted in large language model (LLM)-based agent systems across various domains. In existing frameworks, skills are typically injected into the agent reasoning loop as contextual guidance once matched to a runtime task, enabling specialized task-solving capabilities. We find that this execution paradigm introduces two major sources of redundancy: irrelevant context injection and repeated skill-specific reasoning and planning. To this end, we propose SkillSmith, a boundary-first compiler-runtime framework that compiles skill packages offline into minimal executable interfaces. By extracting fine-grained operational boundaries from skills, SkillSmith enables agents to dynamically access and execute only the relevant components at runtime, thereby minimizing unnecessary context injection and redundant reasoning overhead. In the evaluation on SkillsBench benchmark, SkillSmith reduces solve-stage token usage by 57.44%, thinking iterations by 42.99%, solve time by 50.57% (2.02x faster), and token-proportional monetary cost by 57.44% compared with using raw-skills. Moreover, compiled artifacts produced by a stronger model can be reused by a smaller or more efficient runtime model, improving task accuracy in cases where raw skill interpretation fails. The source code and data are available at https://github.com/AetherHeart-AI/Aeloon.

</details>


### [32] [Fair outputs, Biased Internals: Causal Potency and Asymmetry of Latent Bias in LLMs for High-Stakes Decisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15217)
*Jagdish Tripathy,Marcus Buckmann*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 指令微调语言模型在高风险决策中表现出行为公平性，但内部表征仍保留偏见关联。通过抵押贷款审批实验发现，模型虽无输出偏差，却保留并放大了人口统计学表征。激活干预表明这些压制信息具有决策相关性，可导致决策逆转，且这种潜在偏见具有不对称性，易受对抗性提示和参数高效微调利用。因此，仅关注输出的行为审计不足以保证公平性，需建立结合输出评估与表征分析的双层测试框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究关注模型输出层面的公平性，但忽视了模型内部表征可能仍保留被压制的偏见信息，以及这些信息是否具有因果影响力、是否在不同人口群体间存在不对称性。

Method: 使用开放权重模型进行抵押贷款审批实验，利用仅在种族关联姓名上有所差异的匹配申请样本；通过激活引导和跨层干预技术，检验被压制信息在关键层的决策影响力。

Result: 模型在输出层面无偏见，但内部表征保留并放大了人口统计学表征；被压制信息具有决策相关性，重新注入可导致近乎完全的决策逆转；这种潜在偏见具有不对称性（单向显著而反向几乎无效），且易受对抗性提示和参数高效微调攻击。

Conclusion: 行为审计（仅关注输出）不足以检测模型公平性，公平输出可能掩盖可利用的内部偏见；应建立结合输出评估与表征分析的双层测试框架以加强AI治理。

Abstract: Instruction-tuned language models exhibit behavioural fairness in high-stakes decisions while retaining biased associations in their internal representations. However, whether these suppressed representations can affect model outputs - and whether such causal potency is symmetric across demographic groups - remains unknown. We investigate the use of open-weight models for mortgage underwriting using matched applications that differ only in racially-associated names and reveal a critical disconnect: models show no output-level bias, yet retain and amplify demographic representations across model layers. Through activation steering and novel cross-layer interventions, we demonstrate that this suppressed information is decision-relevant: when reinjected at critical layers, it produces near-complete decision reversals. Critically, this latent bias is asymmetric - steering interventions affect decisions in one demographic direction, while producing minimal effects in reverse - and susceptible to adversarial prompt engineering and parameter-efficient fine-tuning. These findings demonstrate that behavioural audits focused on outputs are insufficient: fair outputs can mask exploitable internal biases. They also motivate dual-layer testing frameworks combining output evaluation with representational analysis for AI governance in high-stakes decisions.

</details>


### [33] [CAX-Agent: A Lightweight Agent Harness for Reliable APDL Automation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15218)
*Chenying Lin,Yichen Hai,Yi He,Ran Wang,Haiyan Qiang,Liang Yu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出CAX-Agent，一种用于MAPDL有限元仿真的轻量级Agent编排框架，通过三层架构（LLM服务层、Agent编排层、求解器后端）和恢复策略梯级（从确定性规则修补到模型驱动再生再到上下文增强和人工干预）解决大语言模型在工程仿真中的可靠性问题。实验表明，纯模型驱动的恢复策略在任务完成率（0.9267）、任务得分（3.59/4）、总分（9.16/10）和零干预率（0.84）上显著优于纯规则恢复和无恢复策略，效应量巨大（Cliff's delta 0.81-0.87）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型直接用于MAPDL有限元仿真时缺乏结构化执行控制、工具封装和故障恢复机制，导致输出不一致、任务失败频发，亟需一种领域特定的编排中间件来管理工具生命周期、工作流状态和恢复升级。

Method: 提出CAX-Agent三层架构：LLM服务层、Agent编排层（核心为恢复梯级策略）和求解器后端。恢复梯级从确定性规则修补→模型驱动再生→上下文增强→人工干预逐级升级。实验设计：在50个标准结构基准上，对三种恢复策略（无恢复、仅规则、仅模型）各重复3次（共450次），由两名独立评审员盲评，使用Cohen's kappa评估一致性，Cliff's delta衡量效应量。

Result: 模型驱动恢复策略在各项指标上均最优：完成率0.9267（vs 规则0.7733、无恢复0.6933），任务得分3.59/4（vs 3.17/4、2.74/4），总分9.16/10（vs 7.03/10、5.60/10），零干预率0.84（vs 0.00、0.00）。效应量Cliff's delta为0.81-0.87，评审一致性较高（加权Cohen's kappa=0.84，96%评分对差值≤1分）。

Conclusion: 模型驱动的恢复策略在MAPDL仿真自动化中显著优于规则驱动和无恢复策略，但基准采用刻意简化的几何形状以隔离恢复策略效应，结论的泛化性有待更广泛的验证。

Abstract: Large language models deployed for MAPDL finite-element simulation face practical reliability challenges: without structured execution control, tool encapsulation, and fault recovery, outputs may be inconsistent and task failures are common. The Agent Harness paradigm addresses this by inserting domain-specific orchestration middleware that manages tool lifecycles, workflow state, and recovery escalation. This paper presents the architecture of CAX-Agent, a lightweight agent harness purpose-built for MAPDL automation, and empirically evaluates one of its core components -- the recovery policy.CAX-Agent organizes execution into three layers -- LLM service, agent harness, and solver backend -- with a recovery ladder that escalates from deterministic rule patching through model-driven regeneration to context enrichment and human intervention. We evaluate three recovery strategies (no_recovery, rule_only, and model_only) on 50 standard structural benchmarks with three repeated runs per strategy (450 case-runs total). Two independent human raters score task completion under blind conditions; inter-rater agreement is strong (quadratic weighted Cohen's kappa = 0.84, 96 percent of score pairs within one point). Model_only achieves the best completion rate (0.9267), task score (3.59/4), total score (9.16/10), and zero-intervention rate (0.84), outperforming rule_only (0.7733, 3.17/4, 7.03/10, 0.00) and no_recovery (0.6933, 2.74/4, 5.60/10, 0.00) with large effect sizes (Cliff's delta = 0.81-0.87). The benchmark uses deliberately simple geometries to isolate recovery-policy effects; we discuss the scope of these findings and directions for broader validation.

</details>


### [34] [NOVA: Fundamental Limits of Knowledge Discovery Through AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15219)
*Salman Avestimehr,Ken Duffy,Muriel Médard*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: NOVA框架将AI迭代自改进建模为知识空间上的自适应采样过程，识别了四种失败模式，揭示了污染陷阱，并证明了在Zipf律假设下累积发现成本服从Θ(c_gen D^α)的标度律，同时形式化了人类增强的价值边界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究AI系统能否通过迭代自改进发现真正的新知识，以及这一过程需要付出何种代价。

Method: 提出NOVA框架，将"生成-验证-积累-重训练"循环建模为知识空间上的自适应采样过程；分析失败模式；利用Good-Turing估计和Zipf律进行理论分析。

Result: 识别了四种失败模式（污染、遗忘、探索失败、接受失败）；发现污染陷阱：当易发现知识耗尽时，新有效工件的模型质量下降，小假阳率也会导致无效工件更快进入知识库；证明了在尾等价假设下，发现D个不同真知识的累积生成成本为Θ(c_gen D^α)。

Conclusion: AI系统在自改进中面临根本性的发现极限和污染风险，人类专家输入在自主探索障碍处最有价值。

Abstract: Can AI systems discover genuinely new knowledge through iterative self improvement, and if so, at what cost? We introduce the NOVA framework, which models the common ``generate, verify, accumulate, retrain'' loop as an adaptive sampling process over a knowledge space. We identify sufficient conditions under which accumulated genuine knowledge eventually covers a finite domain, and show how their violations produce distinct failure modes: contamination, forgetting, exploration failure, and acceptance failure. We then analyze imperfect verification and identify a contamination trap: as easy-to-find knowledge is exhausted, the model mass assigned to new valid artifacts shrinks, so even small false-positive rates can cause invalid artifacts to enter the knowledge base faster than genuine discoveries. We clarify that Good--Turing estimation is a local batch-diversity diagnostic, not an estimator of the historically undiscovered valid mass that governs long-term discovery. Under a separate tail-equivalence assumption relating the model's effective discovery distribution to a Zipf law with exponent $α>1$, we prove that the cumulative generation cost required to obtain $D$ distinct genuine discoveries satisfies $R_{\mathrm{cum}}(D)=Θ(c_{\mathrm{gen}}D^α)$, where $c_{\mathrm{gen}}$ is the per-candidate generation cost. This scaling law quantifies asymptotic diminishing returns as the discovery frontier advances. Finally, we formalize human amplification through guidance, generation, and verification, explaining why expert input is most valuable near autonomous exploration barriers.

TL;DR: 提出ICRL框架，通过强化学习联合训练求解器与评论家，使模型内化自我批评能力，在无需外部批评的情况下提升自身性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法中，模型依赖外部批评才能正确回答问题，移除批评后性能下降；批评者无法自我进化，限制了迭代提升。

Method: ICRL：基于共享主干联合训练求解器和评论家；评论家依据求解器后续性能增益获得奖励；引入分布校准重加权比处理分布偏移；角色分组优势估计稳定联合优化。

Result: 以Qwen3-4B/8B为骨干，在智能体和数学推理任务上，代理任务平均比GRPO高6.4分，数学推理高7.0分；8B评论家性能可媲美32B评论家且使用更少token。

Abstract: Large language model-based agents make mistakes, yet critique can often guide the same model toward correct behavior. However, when critique is removed, the model may fail again on the same query, indicating that it has not internalized the critique's guidance into its underlying capability. Meanwhile, a frozen critic cannot improve its feedback quality over time, limiting the potential for iterative self-improvement. To address this, we propose learning to internalize self-critique with reinforcement learning(ICRL), a novel framework that jointly trains a solver and a critic from a shared backbone to convert critique-induced success into unassisted solver ability. The critic is rewarded based on the solver's subsequent performance gain, incentivizing actionable feedback. To address the distribution shift between critique-conditioned and critique-free behavior, ICRL introduces a distribution-calibration re-weighting ratio that selectively transfers critique-guided improvements compatible with the solver's own prompt distribution. Additionally, a role-wise group advantage estimation stabilizes joint optimization across the two roles. Together, these mechanisms ensure that the solver learns to improve itself without external critique, rather than becoming dependent on critique-conditioned behavior. We evaluate ICRL on diverse benchmarks spanning agentic and mathematical reasoning tasks, using Qwen3-4B and Qwen3-8B as backbones. Results show consistent improvements, with average gains of 6.4 points over GRPO on agentic tasks, and 7.0 points on mathematical reasoning. Notably, the learned 8B critic is comparable to 32B critics while using substantially fewer tokens. The code is available at https://github.com/brick-pid/ICRL.

  We define the model, instantiate it over an OpenKedge-based governed mutation substrate, and show how it maps onto cloud-native environments. Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) still struggle with the rigorous reasoning demands of hard competitive programming. While recent multi-agent frameworks attempt to bridge this reliability gap, they remain fundamentally stateless: they rely on static retrieval and discard the valuable problem-solving and debugging experience gained from previous tasks. To address this, we present Solvita, an agentic evolution framework that enables continuous learning without requiring weight updates to the underlying LLM. Solvita reorganizes problem-solving into a closed-loop system of strategy selection, program synthesis, certified supervision, and targeted hacking, executed by four specialized agents: Planner, Solver, Oracle, and Hacker. This allows the agents to dynamically route future queries based on past successes and failures, effectively accumulating transferable reasoning experience over time. Abstract: LLM-driven program evolution has emerged as a powerful tool for automated scientific discovery, yet existing frameworks offer no principled guide for designing their individual components and provide no guarantee that the search converges. ### [40] [Context Pruning for Coding Agents via Multi-Rubric Latent Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15315)
*Jingjing Wang,Xiwen Chen,Wenhui Zhu,Huayu Li,Zhengxiao He,Feiyang Cai,Ana S. Carreon-Rascon,Xuanzhao Dong,Feng Luo*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: LaMR是一个将代码相关性分解为语义证据和依赖支持两个可解释维度的结构化剪枝框架，通过多CRF建模和混合专家门控网络动态聚合，在无需额外标注的情况下实现了比未剪枝全上下文基线更优或相当的代码检索压缩效果，在四个基准测试中节省最多31%的token且性能不降反升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有学习型代码剪枝器使用单目标序列标注器将代码相关性的所有维度压缩为一个分数和一个转移矩阵，导致单一CRF转移先验需要同时服务于语义连续跨度与稀疏结构支持行等异构保留模式，形成了建模瓶颈。

Method: 将代码相关性分解为语义证据（semantic evidence）和依赖支持（dependency support）两个可解释维度，每个维度由专用CRF建模，具有维度特定的转移动态；通过混合专家门控网络根据查询动态加权各维度发射分数；融合后的发射分数经最终CRF层产生聚合的保留或剪枝决策；通过AST程序分析从现有训练语料中自动推导多维度标签，同时去噪教师模型的二元标签。

Result: 在SWE-Bench Verified、SWE-QA、LCC、LongCodeQA四个基准上，LaMR在16项成对多轮比较中赢得12项；在多轮智能体任务上节省最多31%的token；在单轮任务上Exact Match提升最多+3.5；通过去噪上下文，性能经常得到提升，剩余下降微乎其微。

Conclusion: 通过分解相关性维度并分别建模，LaMR有效过滤了干扰噪声，在压缩上下文的同时经常匹配甚至超越未剪枝的全上下文基线，证明了结构化多维度剪枝策略的有效性。

Abstract: LLM-powered coding agents spend the majority of their token budget reading repository files, yet much of the retrieved code is irrelevant to the task at hand. Existing learned pruners compress this context with a single-objective sequence labeler, collapsing all facets of code relevance into one score and one transition matrix. We show that this formulation creates a modeling bottleneck: a single CRF transition prior must serve heterogeneous retention patterns, including contiguous semantic spans and sparse structural support lines. We propose LaMR (Latent Multi-Rubric), a structured pruning framework that decomposes code relevance into two interpretable quality dimensions, semantic evidence and dependency support, each modeled by a dedicated CRF with dimension-specific transition dynamics. A mixture-of-experts gating network dynamically weights the per-rubric emissions conditioned on the query, and a final CRF layer on the fused emissions produces the aggregate keep-or-prune decision. To supervise each dimension without additional annotation cost, we derive multi-rubric labels from the existing training corpus via AST-based program analysis, simultaneously denoising the teacher's binary labels. By effectively filtering distracting noise, LaMR frequently matches or even outperforms unpruned full-context baselines. Experiments on four benchmarks (SWE-Bench Verified, SWE-QA, LCC, LongCodeQA) show that LaMR wins 12 of 16 head-to-head multi-turn comparisons. It saves up to 31% more tokens on multi-turn agent tasks and improves Exact Match by up to +3.5 on single-turn tasks, while performance is frequently enhanced by denoising the context, and any remaining drops are marginal.

Motivation: 目标识别是一种溯因推理任务，天然更适合LLM的优势（评估与世界知识的一致性而非生成新动作序列），因此可作为检验LLM基础规划知识的原理性基准。

Result: LLM在目标识别上的表现不均衡：部分模型随观测证据增多精度提升，接近地标方法的水平；另一些模型无论证据多少都固守世界知识先验。

Conclusion: 模型间的差异根源在于证据整合能力的不同而非领域熟悉度，目标识别可定位为评估LLM基础规划知识的原则性基准任务。

Abstract: Large language models have recently reached near-parity with classical planners on well-known planning domains, yet this competence relies on world-knowledge exploitation rather than genuine symbolic reasoning. Goal recognition is a complementary abductive task structurally better suited to LLM strengths: it consists of evaluating consistency with world knowledge rather than generating novel action sequences. This paper provides the first systematic zero-shot evaluation of frontier LLMs as goal recognisers on key classical PDDL benchmarks. Our results show that LLM competence on goal recognition is uneven: some models scale with evidence and approach landmark-based accuracy at full observations, while others remain anchored to world-knowledge priors regardless of how much evidence accumulates. Qualitative analysis of model reasoning traces reveals that this divergence reflects a fundamental difference in evidence integration rather than domain familiarity. These findings position goal recognition as a principled benchmark for the foundational planning knowledge of LLMs.

### [42] [Belief Engine: Configurable and Inspectable Stance Dynamics in Multi-Agent LLM Deliberation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15343)
*Joshua C. Yang,Maurice Flechtner,Damian Dailisan,Michiel A. Bakker*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出Belief Engine (BE)，一个可审计的信念更新层，将信念建模为命题上的证据状态并通过标量立场暴露。BE将论证提取到结构化记忆中，使用由证据吸收率u和先验锚定a控制的对数几率规则更新立场。实验表明，BE能可靠地塑造立场动态，同时保留证据级更新轨迹，并在DEBATE人类辩论数据集上最好地重建了立场随证据变化的参与者。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: Belief Engine将"信念"定义为命题上的证据状态并以标量立场形式暴露。它提取论证到结构化记忆中，通过由证据吸收率u和先验锚定a控制的对数几率规则更新立场。跨多个基础LLM进行参数扫描，验证这些控制参数能可靠塑造立场动态并保留证据级更新轨迹。

Result: 在DEBATE人类辩论数据集上，BE最好地重建了最终立场遵循提取证据的参与者；对于立场稳定或与证据相反的案例，则指向锚定效应或提取证据流之外的因素。

Conclusion: BE为研究基于证据的协商提供了可配置的基础设施，使得开放性、承诺、收敛和分歧等行为可联系到明确的更新假设，而非隐藏的提示效应。

Abstract: LLM-based agents are increasingly used to simulate deliberative interactions such as negotiation, conflict resolution, and multi-turn opinion exchange. Yet generated transcripts often do not reveal why an agent's stance changes: movement may reflect evidence uptake, anchoring, role drift, echoing, or changed prompt and retrieval context. We introduce the Belief Engine (BE), an auditable belief-update layer that treats "belief" as an evidential state over a proposition and exposes it as scalar stance. BE extracts arguments into structured memory and updates stance with a log-odds rule controlled by evidence uptake u and prior anchoring a. Across multiple base LLMs, parameter sweeps show that these controls reliably shape stance dynamics while preserving an evidence-level update trail. On DEBATE, a human deliberation dataset with pre/post opinions, BE best reconstructs participants whose final stance follows extracted evidence; stable and evidence-opposed cases instead point to anchoring or factors outside the extracted evidence stream. BE provides configurable infrastructure for studying evidence-grounded deliberation, where openness, commitment, convergence, and disagreement can be tied to explicit update assumptions rather than hidden prompt effects.

### [43] [Ensemble Monitoring for AI Control: Diverse Signals Outweigh More Compute](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15377)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建12个GPT-4.1-Mini监控器，采用提示工程和微调两种策略；在编程任务（候选解决方案通过标准测试但对抗性输入失败）上评估；通过集成多样化监控器信号来改进误对齐行为检测。

We show that combining signals from diverse monitors into an ensemble improves detection of misaligned actions. We build 12 GPT-4.1-Mini monitors using both prompting and fine-tuning strategies. We evaluate them on coding tasks where candidate solutions pass standard tests but fail on adversarial inputs. In this setting, diverse ensembles outperform both individual monitors and homogeneous ensembles. Our best 3-monitor ensemble achieves 2.4x greater detection performance gain compared to an ensemble composed of three identical monitors, with the same ensemble performing strongly on an independent dataset. We contend that these results show that diversity - not scale - drives gains. The best ensembles combine strong individual performance with low correlation between monitors. Furthermore, fine-tuned monitors appear in every top-performing ensemble and maintain this advantage on out-of-distribution attack types, suggesting that fine-tuning enables detection capabilities that prompting alone does not elicit. Abstract: While AI agents are rapidly advancing from isolated tools to interactive collaborators, data-driven human-machine teaming (HMT) methods remain costly in their reliance on human interaction data across domains, teammates, and team sizes. Zero-shot coordination (ZSC) addresses this bottleneck by simulating diverse partner populations to approximate how unseen partners might behave. However, partner coverage alone is insufficient as team settings scale and communication becomes degraded. To remedy this deficiency, we propose Influence-Based Team Steering (IBTS), a framework that uses influence shaping to incentivize agents to discover diverse, high-performing team interaction patterns and further steers ongoing trajectories toward stronger learned coordination modes. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多项式不等式的自动证明面临可扩展性挑战：纯符号方法因代数操作和中间表达式膨胀而难以扩展；LLM引导方法在处理少变量竞赛题时有进展，但仍无法解决多变量、高维度的可扩展性问题。

Method: 提出NSPI框架，包含两个核心阶段：(1) LLM生成近似多项式平方和（SOS）分解作为猜想；(2) 通过符号计算精化该近似分解，得到精确的多项式SOS表示，从而直接证明目标不等式。最终在Lean定理证明器中完成机器可验证的证明。
