### [196] [Mind Dreamer: Untethering Imagination via Active Latent Intervention on Latent Manifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16030)
*Shaojun Xu,Xiaoling Zhou,Yihan Lin,Yapeng Meng,Xinglong Ji,Luping Shi,Rong Zhao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出Mind Dreamer (MD)框架，通过主动潜在干预（ALI）解决模型强化学习中策略优化滞后于世界模型流形发现的学习不对称问题。MD从学习生成器而非历史缓冲区采样初始状态，利用对抗生成器合成非连续潜在跳跃至认知盲区，并推导了中继值函数（RVF）和中继不确定性函数（RUF）来解决跨空间断裂的信用分配问题。理论证明不确定性跨不连续传播需要二次折扣γ²。实验在DeepMind Control Suite上平均加速1.67倍，稀疏奖励任务达8.8倍。

Method: Mind Dreamer (MD) 框架包含三个核心组件：(1) 主动潜在干预（ALI）：通过学习生成器$s_0 \sim p_{gen}(\cdot)$采样初始状态，替代从历史缓冲区的采样，利用对抗生成器合成非连续潜在跳跃到物理可行但认知挑战性的盲点；(2) 中继值函数（RVF）和中继不确定性函数（RUF）：将合成锚点视为反事实中间状态，通过贝尔曼形式传播实用价值和认知价值；(3) 跨不连续不确定性传播需要二次折扣γ²的理论推导。

Result: 在DeepMind Control Suite上，MD相比DreamerV3实现了1.67倍的平均加速，在稀疏奖励任务中达到8.8倍。理论分析表明MD近似于一个方差最小化重要性采样器，扩大流形谱隙，减少到达关键瓶颈状态的首达时间。

Conclusion: Mind Dreamer通过主动潜在干预突破马尔可夫连续性约束，有效解决了MBRL中的历史系链问题，揭示了跨不连续不确定性传播的二次折扣规律，在复杂控制任务中显著提升了样本效率。

Abstract: Model-Based Reinforcement Learning (MBRL) leverages latent imagination for sample efficiency, yet remains constrained by Historical Tethering: imagination is typically initialized from observed states. This creates a learning asymmetry, where the world model's manifold discovery outpaces the policy's sparse-reward optimization. We propose Mind Dreamer (MD), a framework that operationalizes Active Latent Intervention (ALI) to transcend Markovian continuity. MD reformulates discovery as the minimization of a global Relay Manifold Expected Free Energy (R-EFE); by sampling initial states from a learned generator $s_0 \sim p_{gen}(\cdot)$ rather than the historical buffer, MD utilizes an adversarial generator to synthesize non-continuous latent jumps to epistemic blind spots that are physically plausible yet cognitively challenging. To resolve the credit assignment paradox across these spatial ruptures, we derive the Relay Value Function (RVF) and Relay Uncertainty Function (RUF). These potentials treat synthesized anchors as counterfactual intermediary states, propagating pragmatic and epistemic value through a principled Bellman-style formulation. Notably, we prove that uncertainty propagation across discontinuities necessitates a quadratic discount $γ^2$, establishing a formal epistemic horizon. Theoretically, MD approximates a variance-minimizing importance sampler that expands the manifold's spectral gap, reducing the hitting time to critical bottleneck states. Empirically, MD achieves a 1.67$\times$ average speedup over DreamerV3 on DeepMind Control Suite, reaching 8.8$\times$ in sparse-reward tasks.

Existing methods relying on global transition matrices underfit these structural patterns, while learning instance-specific matrices remains mathematically intractable. We propose Model-Induced Noise Decoupling (MIND), a theoretically grounded framework addressing this dilemma. We demonstrate that the high-dimensional noise manifold can be decoupled into tractable, subspace-dependent components via Latent Manifold Disentanglement. Specifically, our Latent Decoupling Estimator (LDE) dynamically projects samples into latent structural clusters with consistent error modes, facilitating noise identifiability without ground-truth anchor points. To rigorously evaluate robustness, we adopt a hierarchical protocol: moving from controlled noise on CIFAR-100 to a structural stress test on large-scale real-world 3D datasets (S3DIS, ScanNet), where error patterns explicitly couple with geometric manifolds. ### [199] [Multi-Fidelity Flow Matching: Cascaded Refinement of PDE Solutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16118)
*Sipeng Chen,Junliang Liu,Hewei Tang,Shibo Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出多保真流匹配（MFFM），一种用于参数化PDE解的级联精化框架。通过将条件流匹配中的源分布校准为数据驱动的低保真到高保真残差尺度（含局部高斯模糊相关性），并将速度网络以低保真解为条件，实现残差精化。多分辨率级联在相邻保真度间独立应用相同结构，经逐级流匹配预训练后，端到端微调级联模型，实现每级一次速度评估的最优推理。在8个基准测试（超分辨率和时空预测任务）上验证了有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有条件流匹配通常使用默认各向同性先验作为源分布，未充分利用数据可校准特性。本文旨在利用可校准源分布，设计一种高效的多保真度级联精化框架，以加速参数化PDE求解过程。

Method: 1. 将条件流匹配的源分布校准为低保真到高保真残差的经验分布，并引入局部高斯模糊相关性；2. 速度网络以低保真解为条件，简化残差精化任务；3. 构建多分辨率级联结构，相邻保真度间独立应用相同框架；4. 逐级流匹配预训练后，端到端微调级联模型，使用确定性单步展开实现每级一次速度评估的最优推理。

Result: 在8个基准测试上验证了MFFM的有效性，包括2个超分辨率问题和6个来自PDEBench、The Well和FNO Navier-Stokes数据集的时空预测任务。结果表明，通过L次确定性网络评估即可达到最细网格精度。

Conclusion: MFFM是一种学习版的多重网格精化方法，通过可校准的源分布和条件化设计，显著提升了参数化PDE求解的效率，实现了高效的多保真度级联精化。

Abstract: The source distribution in conditional flow matching is a design parameter that can be calibrated to data, not a default isotropic prior. We exploit this in Multi-Fidelity Flow Matching (MFFM), a cascade refinement framework for parametric PDE solutions: the source is calibrated to the empirical low-to-high-fidelity residual scale with local Gaussian-blur correlation, and the velocity network is conditioned on the low-fidelity solution. Conditioning makes the residual refinement problem substantially easier than unconditional field generation, while residual-calibrated source noise improves the flow-matching training geometry. A multi-resolution cascade applies the same construction independently between adjacent fidelities. After level-wise flow-matching pretraining, we fine-tune the composed cascade end-to-end with a deterministic one-step rollout, which makes one velocity evaluation per cascade level the optimized operating point at inference. The result is a learned analog of multigrid refinement that reaches the finest grid in $L$ deterministic network evaluations per query. We validate MFFM on eight benchmarks: two super-resolution problems and six spatiotemporal forecasting tasks from PDEBench, The Well, and the FNO Navier--Stokes dataset.

### [200] [Learn Where Outcomes Diverge: Efficient VLA RL via Probabilistic Chunk Masking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16154)
*Vaidehi Bagaria,Nikshep Grampurohit,Pulkit Verma*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出概率性分块掩码（PCM），一种针对GRPO的即插即用改进方法。PCM基于成功-失败动作方差代理每阶段梯度方差，仅对轨迹中少数概率性选中的语义阶段进行梯度计算，在LIBERO基准上实现2.38倍加速、4.8倍梯度更新加速和60%峰值激活内存降低，且不损失最终成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于GRPO的VLA策略强化学习后训练中，梯度计算占总时间约78%，是主导开销。而GRPO对轨迹所有分块分配相同优势，导致大量梯度计算浪费在策略已能处理的阶段。因此需要一种方法将梯度计算集中在真正能产生学习信号的阶段。

Method: 提出Probabilistic Chunk Masking (PCM)：1) 使用成功-失败动作方差作为每阶段梯度方差的代理指标；2) 按语义阶段（chunk）在线更新保留概率；3) 对每个轨迹，仅对固定预算的随机子集分块进行反向传播，其余分块被掩码掉。PCM无需奖励模型或可学习的critic。

Result: 在三个LIBERO基准上，PCM匹配标准GRPO的最终成功率，同时实现2.38倍端到端加速、4.8倍梯度更新加速、60%更低的峰值激活内存，且仅对少于20%的轨迹分块进行反向传播。

Conclusion: PCM通过识别并集中计算资源于高信息量的轨迹阶段，在不牺牲策略性能的前提下显著降低VLA后训练的计算开销，揭示了GRPO中梯度计算浪费的本质原因并提供了一种轻量级解决方案。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) allows vision-language-action (VLA) policies to generalize beyond their training distribution by optimizing directly for task success, but post-training is computationally expensive. A natural response has been to speed rollout collection through faster simulators and world models. In GRPO-based VLA RL, we find that the dominant cost lies elsewhere: gradient computation accounts for approximately 78% of wall-clock time per step in our runs, while rollout collection accounts for only 21%. Gradient cost dominates because much of this computation is spent on phases that contribute little to learning. GRPO's learning signal is driven by advantage variance: only phases where successful and failed rollouts diverge produce learning signal. However, GRPO assigns the same advantage to every chunk in a rollout. As a result, actor-update compute is spent uniformly across the trajectory, including phases the policy already handles after pre-training and supervised fine-tuning. This paper presents Probabilistic Chunk Masking (PCM), a drop-in modification to GRPO that allocates gradient computation to a small, probabilistically selected subset of chunks per trajectory. PCM scores semantic phases using success-failure action variance, a rollout-derived proxy for per-phase gradient variance, and samples a fixed chunk budget with online-updated phase-level keep probabilities. We formalize per-phase gradient variance as the quantity determines where gradient computation is useful and show that success-failure action variance provides a measurable proxy for it. PCM requires no reward model or learned critic. On three LIBERO benchmarks, PCM matches the final success rate of standard GRPO while achieving 2.38 times wall-clock speedup, 4.8 times faster gradient updates, and 60% lower peak activation memory, while backpropagating through fewer than 20% of trajectory chunks.

</details>

Abstract: Despite their ubiquity, variational autoencoders (VAEs) inherently suffer from posterior collapse, a failure mode in which latent variables are effectively ignored. This failure arises because explicit prior imposition drives optimization toward loss landscape regions corresponding to uninformative latent representations. Here, we introduce Entropic Autoencoders (EAEs), a framework in which reconstruction loss is the only explicit objective, and entropy generates the latent variables' prior implicitly through a free energy-minimizing ensemble of encoders. This ensemble biases learning toward high-volume regions of near-optimal solutions, while decoder updates direct the search trajectories toward informative latent representations. We demonstrate that EAEs mitigate posterior collapse by learning non-Gaussian, multimodal latent distributions that yield diverse, data-consistent generations and preserve different forms of underlying structure in the data. As a proof-of-concept, we show that an EAE captures a superposition of the known low-dimensional dynamics of a reaction-diffusion process. Then, we show that an EAE identifies implicit categorical distinctions in MNIST latent representations, and displays a hierarchical understanding of facial structure on the CelebA dataset, from an "all-human" face to individual-dependent features.

### [202] [BAPR: Bayesian amnesic piecewise-robust reinforcement learning for non-stationary continuous control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16170)
*Yifan Zhang,Liang Zheng*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: BAPR将贝叶斯在线变化检测(BOCD)与鲁棒集成强化学习相结合，提出一种分段鲁棒控制框架。其核心是冻结信念分布加权的模态条件Bellman算子凸组合（BAPR算子），被证明是γ-收缩算子；通过Lean 4形式化验证了收缩的尖锐边界（γ+λΔ≥1时失效）。BOCD驱动自适应保守机制：检测到变化点后策略最大保守，随后随置信度平滑放松，检测延迟O(log(1/δ))。所有结果均在Lean 4中形式化验证（1,145行代码，22个机器验证定理）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真实世界控制系统常呈现分段平稳特性（长时间稳定后突然发生模态切换）。标准鲁棒强化学习方法面临根本性困境：全局保守策略在稳定期浪费性能，而局部自适应策略在未检测到模态变化时可能导致灾难性失败。需要一种能自动检测变化并自适应调整保守程度的控制框架。

Method: 1) 提出BAPR算子：模态条件Bellman算子的凸组合，权重为冻结的信念分布；2) 证明该算子是γ-收缩算子，并推导出当信念依赖Q函数时收缩因子的尖锐边界（γ+λΔ）；3) 导出组件式的形式化误差界，约束切换后恢复行为；4) BOCD模块驱动自适应保守机制（变化后最大保守，随置信度增长平滑放松，检测延迟O(log(1/δ))）；5) 上下文条件模块通过RMDM损失训练模态感知表示（训练时使用模拟器模态ID，部署时无需模态标签）。

Result: 1) BAPR算子是γ-收缩算子（形式化证明）；2) 发现收缩的尖锐边界：当信念依赖Q函数时，收缩因子变为γ+λΔ，且当γ+λΔ≥1时收缩失败；3) 导出组件式形式化误差界，约束切换后恢复；4) 所有结果在Lean 4中形式化验证（1,145行代码，22个定理，无sorry）；5) BOCD实现自适应保守机制，检测延迟O(log(1/δ))。

Conclusion: BAPR通过统一BOCD与鲁棒集成RL，有效解决了分段平稳环境中全局保守与局部自适应之间的根本矛盾。形式化验证保证了理论结果的可靠性。该方法在训练时利用模态ID学习模态感知表示，部署时无需模态标签，具有良好的实用性。

Abstract: Real-world control systems frequently operate under \emph{piecewise stationary} conditions, where dynamics remain stable for extended periods before undergoing abrupt regime changes. Standard robust RL methods face a fundamental dilemma: a globally conservative policy wastes performance during stable periods, while a locally adaptive policy risks catastrophic failure when the regime changes undetected.
  We propose \textbf{BAPR} (Bayesian Amnesic Piecewise-Robust SAC), which unifies Bayesian Online Change Detection (BOCD) with robust ensemble RL. The BAPR operator -- a convex combination of mode-conditional Bellman operators weighted by a frozen belief distribution -- is a $γ$-contraction. A complementary counterexample, machine-verified in Lean~4, establishes a \emph{sharp boundary}: when beliefs depend on the Q-function, the contraction factor becomes $γ+ λΔ$ (where $Δ$ is the mode reward gap), and contraction fails exactly when $γ+ λΔ\geq 1$. We derive a \emph{component-wise} formal error budget for the abstract operator -- every component machine-verified -- bounding post-switch recovery; the budget applies to the abstract mode-mixture operator and inherits to the implemented shared-critic algorithm only through the frozen-parameter design intuition. All results are formally verified with no \texttt{sorry} (1,145 lines across 3 Lean~4 files, 22 machine-verified theorems). BOCD drives an adaptive conservatism mechanism: the policy becomes maximally conservative after detected change-points and smoothly relaxes as confidence grows, with detection delay $O(\log(1/δ))$. A context-conditioning module trained via RMDM loss provides mode-aware representations from simulator-provided mode IDs at training time and requires no mode labels at deployment.

</details>


### [203] [Imitation learning for clinical decision support in pediatric ECMO](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16175)
*Fateme Golivand,Michael Skinner,Saurabh Mathur,Ameet Soni,Phillip Reeder,Kristian Kersting,Lakshmi Raman,Sriraam Natarajan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出将儿科ECMO临床决策建模为从轨迹中学习的模仿学习问题（动作不可直接观测），并采用TabPFN方法学习动作模型，在真实儿科ECMO数据上，TabPFN优于XGBoost和MLP等传统基线，可作为强大的临床行为基线用于儿科ECMO决策支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 儿科重症监护中ECMO治疗面临高复杂性和数据稀缺的挑战，现有方法难以有效建模临床干预决策，亟需一种能从观测数据中学习决策行为的方法。

Method: 将临床决策建模为从轨迹中学习的模仿学习问题（动作不可直接观测），采用TabPFN（基于Transformer的表格数据方法）学习动作模型，并与XGBoost、MLP等传统基线进行对比。

Result: 在真实儿科ECMO数据上，TabPFN方法在动作模型学习任务中持续优于XGBoost和MLP等传统基线方法。

Conclusion: TabPFN可作为儿科ECMO决策支持中强有力的临床行为基线，为解决儿科重症监护中的高复杂性和数据稀缺问题提供了有效方案。

Abstract: Pediatric critical care is a dynamic, high-stakes process involving constant monitoring and adjustments in life-saving treatments. Modeling these interventions is crucial for effective decision support. To address the challenges of high complexity and data scarcity in pediatric Extracorporeal Membrane Oxygenation (ECMO), we frame clinical decision-making as learning to act from trajectories, i.e., imitation learning that learns action models from observational data, with a key feature that actions are not directly observed. We consider TabPFN, a recent transformer-based approach for tabular data, and traditional baselines including XGBoost and Multi-Layer Perceptrons(MLPs) on real-world pediatric ECMO data to learn the action models. We find that the TabPFN-based approach consistently outperforms these classical baselines, supporting its use as a strong clinician-behavior baseline for pediatric ECMO decision support.

### [204] [Hypothesis-driven construction of mesoscopic dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16211)
*Zhuoyuan Li,Aiqing Zhu,Qianxiao Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于广义昂萨格原理的介观动力学学习框架，在假设类中预先保证了全局适定性、渐近稳定性、唯一分解可辨识性和离散能量耗散等理论性质，通过数据驱动方式识别具体模型，实验验证了其在连续PDE和微观链模型数据上的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统科学建模依赖固定、实例级别的有效方程和特定方程的分析计算，在多尺度系统等复杂应用中面临巨大挑战，亟需一种新的范式来学习介观动力学。

Method: 基于广义昂萨格原理，构建了一个统一的数学约束假设类，同时涵盖耗散和保守介观动力学；在该假设类中预先建立全局适定性、渐近稳定性、唯一分解可辨识性和离散能量耗散等理论保证，再通过数据驱动方式识别假设类中的具体成员。

Result: 在连续PDE模型数据（作为对照验证）和微观链模型数据（精确介观模型未知）上均验证了框架的有效性，不仅能有效学习动力学，还能提供可解释的底层物理诊断信息。

Conclusion: 该框架作为一种有效的动力学学习方法，同时能够提供对底层物理的可解释诊断，为复杂系统建模提供了新的范式。

Abstract: Traditional scientific modeling typically begins with fixed, instance-wise effective equations and then carries out equation-specific analysis and computation, a procedure that becomes exceptionally challenging in complex applications such as multiscale systems. We propose an alternative paradigm by learning mesoscopic dynamics within a mathematically constrained hypothesis class. Building upon a generalized Onsager principle, we introduce a unified framework encompassing both dissipative and conservative mesoscopic dynamics. We establish uniform and a priori theoretical guarantees, including global well-posedness, asymptotic stability, unique factorization identifiability, and discrete energy dissipation, applicable to all spatio-temporal evolution equations within this hypothesis class prior to all learning stages. Data from each problem instance is then used to guide the identification of members within our hypothesis class, giving rise to accurate, robust and interpretable dynamical models. We empirically validate this framework on both data from continuum PDE models as a check, and on data arising from microscopic chain models for which exact meso-scale models are unknown. The proposed approach not only acts as an effective dynamics learner, but also offers vital interpretable diagnostics of the underlying physics.

### [205] [Dynamics-Level Watermarking of Flow Matching Models with Random Codes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16239)
*Shuchan Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在生成模型动力学层面嵌入水印的方法，通过在流匹配模型的连续动力学（速度场）中添加密钥相关的扰动来编码水印，不影响生成分布质量，并在MNIST和CIFAR-10上验证了可靠性、生成质量保持和密钥安全性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有生成模型水印方法通常嵌入在模型权重或输出中，本文探索一种新的水印嵌入维度——在模型学习的连续动力学过程中嵌入水印，以实现更高的隐蔽性和安全性。

Method: 将水印嵌入流匹配模型的连续动力学（速度场）中，通过连续信道上的随机编码实现：训练时添加密钥相关的扰动，检测时通过黑盒查询恢复消息。扰动设计确保不改变生成分布。

Result: 在MNIST和CIFAR-10数据集上，不同架构下均能可靠恢复水印消息，生成质量保持完好，且在无密钥时解码准确率仅为随机猜测水平。

Conclusion: 在生成模型动力学层面嵌入水印是可行且有效的，既保证了生成质量无损，又实现了安全性（密钥依赖性），为生成模型水印提供了新的研究维度。

Abstract: We introduce a dynamics-level approach to watermarking generative models. Rather than embedding signals into model weights or outputs, we embed the watermark directly into the learned continuous dynamics -- the velocity field of a flow matching model. We formulate this as random coding over a continuous channel: a key-dependent perturbation is added during training, and the message is recovered at detection time from black-box queries. The perturbation is designed to leave the generated distribution unchanged. Experiments on MNIST and CIFAR-10 across different architectures confirm reliable message recovery, preserved generation quality, and chance-level decoding accuracy without the secret key.

</details>
